[Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo") (protégé)[[20]](#cite_note-Moving_Target-20)

[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:Character)

:   "*Of all the things at risk, the loss of an objective reality is perhaps the most dangerous. The death of truth is the ultimate victory of evil. When truth leaves us, when we let it slip away, when it is ripped from our hands, we become vulnerable to the appetite of whatever monster screams the loudest. This chamber's hold on the truth was finally lost on the Ghorman Plaza. What took place yesterday… what happened yesterday on Ghorman was unprovoked genocide. Yes, genocide! And that truth has been exiled from this chamber! And the monster screaming the loudest? The monster we've helped create? The monster who will come for us all soon enough… is Emperor Palpatine!*"
:   ―Mon Mothma denounces [Emperor Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious")[[21]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_the_Rebellion-21)

**Mon Mothma**, also known affectionately as **Double-M**, was a [human](/wiki/Human "Human") [female](/wiki/Gender "Gender") [Chandrilan](/wiki/Chandrilan "Chandrilan") [politician](/wiki/Politics "Politics") and revolutionary leader who was one of the [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic")'s founding members and its [civilian leader](/wiki/Chancellor_(Rebel_Alliance) "Chancellor (Rebel Alliance)"). During the final [decades](/wiki/Standard_decade "Standard decade") of the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") [Era](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era"), Mothma [represented](/wiki/Senator "Senator") her [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld") of [Chandrila](/wiki/Chandrila "Chandrila") in the [Republic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate") and, in this role, was an outspoken advocate of peace and [democracy](/wiki/Democracy "Democracy") during the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), a pan-[galactic](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy") conflict between the Republic and its [splinter state](/wiki/Raxus_Address "Raxus Address"), the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems"). After the [reorganization](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") of the Republic into the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") at the end of the war, Mothma retained her seat in the now-[Imperial Senate](/wiki/Imperial_Senate "Imperial Senate"), but she began organizing underground resistance movements to combat the [Imperial](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") government alongside militant [Luthen Rael](/wiki/Luthen_Rael "Luthen Rael") and fellow senator [Bail Organa](/wiki/Bail_Prestor_Organa "Bail Prestor Organa") of [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan "Alderaan"). After years of leading a double life, Mothma became the impetus for the [official establishment](/wiki/Declaration_of_the_Rebel_Alliance "Declaration of the Rebel Alliance") of the Rebel Alliance by resigning from the Senate, assuming leadership of the newly-established Rebellion. The Rebel Alliance, led by her, [overthrew](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War") the Empire and restored the Old Republic as a nascent [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic"), of which Mothma was its first [Chancellor](/wiki/Chancellor_(New_Republic) "Chancellor (New Republic)").

In accordance with Chandrilan custom, Mothma was [betrothed](/wiki/Marriage "Marriage") to [Perrin Fertha](/wiki/Perrin_Fertha "Perrin Fertha"), and the pair moved to the galactic [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant"), where she began her tenure as senator of her homeworld, forming ties with several fellow progressively-minded senators, including Organa, [Onaconda Farr](/wiki/Onaconda_Farr "Onaconda Farr") of [Rodia](/wiki/Rodia "Rodia"), and later, [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala") of [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo"). Together, they strived to maintain the Republic's democratic ideals and loyalty to the government amidst the burgeoning [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis"). Despite their faction's efforts to alleviate the crisis, the Republic entered the Clone Wars. Mothma and her allies were vehemently opposed to the war and often led efforts to de-escalate the conflict and bring about a diplomatic solution, but they faced opposition from militarist senators and corporate entities. Her faction's peace initiatives and anti-war legislation often saw failure and pushback, such as the [murder](/wiki/Death "Death") of Senator Farr during controversy over a [bid](/wiki/Reduced_military_spending_bill "Reduced military spending bill") to overturn a [military funding increase](/wiki/Republic_military_enhancement_bill "Republic military enhancement bill").

As the war drew to a close, Organa, Mothma, and Amidala [petitioned](/wiki/Petition_of_2,000 "Petition of 2,000") the increasingly-authoritarian [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") to rescind his [executive wartime powers](/wiki/Emergency_Powers_Act "Emergency Powers Act") following the end of the war. To their horror, Palpatine—secretly the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") [Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Sidious—instead declared the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") guilty of [treason](/wiki/Treason "Treason") and announced that he would transform the Republic into an Empire. Under the new regime, Mothma continued to serve in the now-Imperial Senate, and she and her allies did what they could to politically oppose Palpatine's reign, though she also involved herself in underground resistance. Carefully navigating various interests in both the Senate and the Rebellion, Mothma was pitted against numerous individuals, such as political rivals [Ars Dangor](/wiki/Ars_Dangor "Ars Dangor") and [Sly Moore](/wiki/Sly_Moore "Sly Moore"); Perrin, who had grown accustomed to the life of a [consort](/wiki/Consort "Consort"); their [daughter](/wiki/Parent "Parent") [Leida](/wiki/Leida_Mothma "Leida Mothma"), with whom she had an estranged relationship; and Rael, who grew increasingly violent. Mothma, however, found comfort with individuals including Organa, his wife, [Breha](/wiki/Breha_Organa "Breha Organa"), their daughter, [Leia](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo"), her cousin, [Vel Sartha](/wiki/Vel_Sartha "Vel Sartha"), and her childhood friend, [Tay Kolma](/wiki/Tay_Kolma "Tay Kolma"). To hide her involvement with Rael's [rebel network](/wiki/Axis_network "Axis network") from the Empire, Mothma betrothed her daughter to [Stekan Sculdun](/wiki/Stekan_Sculdun "Stekan Sculdun"), son of Chandrilan oligarch [Davo Sculdun](/wiki/Davo_Sculdun "Davo Sculdun").

As the Empire increased its efforts to crack down on various rebel cells, Mothma continued with her struggle but found her influence diminishing and chances for peaceful settlement gone. When the Empire [massacred peaceful protestors](/wiki/Ghorman_Massacre "Ghorman Massacre") on the planet [Ghorman](/wiki/Ghorman "Ghorman"), Mothma [publicly denounced](/wiki/Escape_from_the_Senate "Escape from the Senate") the Empire and resigned from the Senate, with the growing Rebellion [formally unified](/wiki/Declaration_of_the_Rebel_Alliance "Declaration of the Rebel Alliance") as the Alliance to Restore the Republic. The fugitive Mothma began working directly with the Alliance. As the conflict between the Rebellion and the Empire grew, large-scale warfare became inevitable. Upon receiving intel that the Empire was constructing a planet-killing [superweapon](/wiki/Superweapon "Superweapon"), Mothma sanctioned the recruitment of [Jyn Erso](/wiki/Jyn_Erso "Jyn Erso"), who led the [Rogue One](/wiki/Rogue_One "Rogue One") [squadron](/wiki/Squadron "Squadron") in stealing the [Death Star](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station") [plans](/wiki/Death_Star_plans "Death Star plans") during the [Battle of](/wiki/Battle_of_Scarif "Battle of Scarif") [Scarif](/wiki/Scarif "Scarif"). After the [Battle of](/wiki/Battle_of_Yavin "Battle of Yavin") [Yavin](/wiki/Yavin_Prime "Yavin Prime") saw the [battle station](/wiki/Battle_station "Battle station")'s destruction, Mothma [led](/wiki/Commander-in-Chief "Commander-in-Chief") the Alliance through its struggle, helping plan the [Battle of](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor") [Endor](/wiki/Endor "Endor") with the [Alliance High Command](/wiki/Alliance_High_Command "Alliance High Command"), which saw the apparent [death](/wiki/Death "Death") of [Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") Palpatine and left the Empire in chaos.

In Endor's immediate aftermath, the Rebel Alliance restored the Old Republic as the New Republic and resumed the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate") as the [New Republic Senate](/wiki/New_Republic_Senate "New Republic Senate") on Chandrila. Mothma was elected as Chancellor, and intended to do away with the emergency wartime powers she inherited from Palpatine and demilitarize the [New Republic Defense Fleet](/wiki/New_Republic_Defense_Fleet "New Republic Defense Fleet") by ninety percent while leaving the [defense](/wiki/Planetary_defense_forces "Planetary defense forces") of individual [planets](/wiki/Planet "Planet") to themselves. When the war finally came to an end, the Republic signed the [Galactic Concordance](/wiki/Galactic_Concordance "Galactic Concordance") with the Empire, and the Republic passed the [Military Disarmament Act](/wiki/Military_Disarmament_Act "Military Disarmament Act"). The looming prospect of [Grand Admiral](/wiki/Grand_Admiral "Grand Admiral") [Thrawn](/wiki/Mitth%27raw%27nuruodo "Mitth'raw'nuruodo")'s return to the galaxy was a watershed moment in her leadership. The end of Mothma's chancellery brought a close to a period of unity in the Republic, with several political factions, such as the [Centrists](/wiki/Centrists "Centrists") and the [Populists](/wiki/Populists "Populists"), breaking out in disagreement over the best future for the new government.

## Biography[]

### Early life[]

:   "*Wizard! Teen senator takes on Coruscant*"
:   ―Headline of Bormea Today[[22]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-22)

 [![Mothma sat in the Galactic Senate by 32 BBY.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/86/New_Senator_Mothma.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180712095757) [![Mothma sat in the Galactic Senate by 32 BBY.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/86/New_Senator_Mothma.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180712095757)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/86/New_Senator_Mothma.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180712095757) 

Mothma sat in the Galactic Senate by 32 BBY.

 

Mon Mothma was [born](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") around [48 BBY](/wiki/48_BBY "48 BBY")[[2]](#cite_note-Birth_date-2) into a [political](/wiki/Politics "Politics") [family](/wiki/Mothma_family "Mothma family"); her [father](/wiki/Mon_Mothma%27s_father "Mon Mothma's father") was an [arbiter-general](/wiki/Arbiter-general "Arbiter-general") in the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic"), and her [mother](/wiki/Tanis_(Chandrila) "Tanis (Chandrila)") was a [governor](/wiki/Governor "Governor") on their [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld") of [Chandrila](/wiki/Chandrila "Chandrila").[[23]](#cite_note-Rogue_One_Visual_Dictionary-23) She also had at least one cousin, [Vel Sartha](/wiki/Vel_Sartha "Vel Sartha").[[24]](#cite_note-Nobody's_Listening-24)

At the age of fifteen, during the Chandrilan [winter](/wiki/Winter "Winter"), Mothma fell in love, discovered [smashball](/wiki/Smashball "Smashball"), and realized her parents' imperfections. Because of that, she decided to turn her back on her family's political dynasty to become a [historian](/wiki/Historian "Historian").[[8]](#cite_note-Rogue_One_novel-8) In order to discourage her from pursing this career path, her parents arranged for a tour for Mothma, accompanied by her personal tutor, to the obscure ruins of the unpopulated planet of [Phothrell](/wiki/Phothrell "Phothrell"), in hopes that she would become bored. Instead, while exploring the theaters in the [Palace of the High Games Masters](/wiki/Palace_of_the_High_Games_Masters "Palace of the High Games Masters") for a full day, she imagined the holographic game pieces and the crowds, and inquired her tutor many questions he was neither able to answer or inclined to learn about.[[7]](#cite_note-MOF-7)

Around the same [time](/wiki/33_BBY "33 BBY"), Mothma [married](/wiki/Wedding_of_Perrin_Fertha_and_Mon_Mothma "Wedding of Perrin Fertha and Mon Mothma") [Perrin Fertha](/wiki/Perrin_Fertha "Perrin Fertha"), a fellow Chandrilan.[[10]](#cite_note-Narkina_5-10) By the next [summer](/wiki/Summer "Summer"), however, her moment of rebellion had been forgotten, and she had returned to politics, both because of family pressures and a genuine love of governance.[[8]](#cite_note-Rogue_One_novel-8) Around [32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY "32 BBY"),[[25]](#cite_note-MOFSenateJoinDate-25) she joined the Republic's [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate"),[[13]](#cite_note-Queen's_Shadow-13) becoming one of the youngest [senators](/wiki/Senator "Senator") to date.[[23]](#cite_note-Rogue_One_Visual_Dictionary-23) At sixteen, Mothma and Perrin, having been married for about a year, moved to Coruscant together, with Mothma serving as senator.[[10]](#cite_note-Narkina_5-10)

Months after their wedding, they carried a passionate and spiteful romance. At the age of twenty, Fertha and Mothma had a falling out and decided to that there would be no children, no shared bed, and no questions between them. At the age of twenty-four, they grew closer, despite previous periods of varying closeness and distance in the relationship, eventually arriving at an equilibrium[[7]](#cite_note-MOF-7) in [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"),[[26]](#cite_note-MOFDate-26) in which they lived separate lives, while maintaining some degree of communication.[[7]](#cite_note-MOF-7)

In [28 BBY](/wiki/28_BBY "28 BBY"),[[27]](#cite_note-QS_Date-27) Mothma spoke at the first senate meeting attended by Senator [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala") of the [Chommell sector](/wiki/Chommell_sector "Chommell sector") as well as several other new senators. Mothma was initially skeptical of Amidala due to her decision to call a vote of no confidence against former [Chancellor](/wiki/Chancellor "Chancellor") [Finis Valorum](/wiki/Finis_Valorum "Finis Valorum") during the [Invasion of Naboo](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo") thus putting the needs of her home world of [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo") above the needs of the [galaxy](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") as a whole.[[13]](#cite_note-Queen's_Shadow-13) Although a dedicated and passionate believer in the Republic, Mothma was aware of its shortcomings and threats the Republic faced.[[28]](#cite_note-HC_40-28) Around this time, Mothma became suspicious of her fellow senator, [Mina Bonteri](/wiki/Mina_Bonteri "Mina Bonteri") of [Onderon](/wiki/Onderon "Onderon"), and hosted a party where Mothma staged a distraction so that she could discuss the matter with her allies Senator [Bail Organa](/wiki/Bail_Prestor_Organa "Bail Prestor Organa") of [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan "Alderaan") and Senator [Onaconda Farr](/wiki/Onaconda_Farr "Onaconda Farr") of [Rodia](/wiki/Rodia "Rodia") in Mothma's [gardens](/wiki/Garden "Garden") while unknowingly being watched by Senator Amidala.[[13]](#cite_note-Queen's_Shadow-13)

Mothma was a member of Organa's [committee for transportation of construction materials](/wiki/Committee_for_transportation_of_construction_materials "Committee for transportation of construction materials") along with Amidala and Farr. Following her eventual alliance with Amidala she used her contacts to stop the [TriNebulon News](/wiki/TriNebulon_News "TriNebulon News") from publishing negative stories on her.[[13]](#cite_note-Queen's_Shadow-13) Mothma eventually became one of Amidala's closest allies but not one of her closest friends.[[29]](#cite_note-Queen's_Hope-29) Eventually, Mothma became one of Amidala's friends and mentors, as Mothma believed that Amidala was one of the best hopes for preserving the Republic. Mothma was one of the most steadfast supporters for peace, and was widely respected throughout the Republic.[[30]](#cite_note-Join_the_Battle-30)

### The Clone Wars and the death of the Republic[]

#### An advocate for peace[]

 [![Mon Mothma represented the planet Chandrila in the Galactic Senate during the Clone Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/45/Mon_Mothma_in_the_Senate.png/revision/latest?cb=20151227040726) [![Mon Mothma represented the planet Chandrila in the Galactic Senate during the Clone Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/45/Mon_Mothma_in_the_Senate.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20151227040726)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/45/Mon_Mothma_in_the_Senate.png/revision/latest?cb=20151227040726) 

Mon Mothma represented the planet Chandrila in the Galactic Senate during the Clone Wars.

 

Joining the senate at a critical time, the [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis") grew to being on the verge of all out war. As part of [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Sheev Palpatine's](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") [Loyalist Committee](/wiki/Loyalist_Committee "Loyalist Committee"), Mothma continued to work closely with Senators Amidala and Organa. Together, they worked to oppose the arming of the Republic and the increasing calls for war against the newly formed [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems").[[28]](#cite_note-HC_40-28) As a member of the Loyalists, Mothma and the other senators were tasked to maintain the Republic's integrity.[[1]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-1) When an [investigation](/wiki/Dogfight_over_Geonosis "Dogfight over Geonosis") by the [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi")[[31]](#cite_note-Episode_II-31) on [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis") revealed that the Confederacy, also known as the Separatists, had already created a large [droid](/wiki/Droid "Droid") military force and a [clone](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") [army](/wiki/Army "Army") was discovered on [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino") and previously commissioned secretly by a Jedi,[[28]](#cite_note-HC_40-28) the galaxy plunged into the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), beginning with the [First Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis").[[31]](#cite_note-Episode_II-31)

Although Mothma and the Loyalist Committee seemed out of step with the new realities of the conflict, they continued to work towards a peaceful solution.[[28]](#cite_note-HC_40-28) Mothma became an outspoken opponent of the war with the Separatists, and along with friends and allies, like Amidala and Organa, came to fear that the Republic's push to defeat the Separatists made it blind to the toll that the war would take on the Republic. She warned that wartime measures, such as the increasing scope of the emergency powers that the Galactic Senate gave the chancellor, were a threat to democracy. It was the desire of Mothma and her allies to find a peaceful solution to the Clone Wars, and Mothma served as a mentor to Amidala as the young senator became one of the leading advocates for peace in the Republic.[[32]](#cite_note-Mon_Mothma_Bio_Gallery-32)

During the [Battle of Malastare](/wiki/Battle_of_Malastare "Battle of Malastare"), the Grand Army of the Republic discovered a creature known as the [Zillo Beast](/wiki/Zillo_Beast "Zillo Beast") that dwelled underneath the surface of the planet [Malastare](/wiki/Malastare "Malastare"). Having been given a way to the surface by the bombardments during the battle, the Zillo Beast fought against the Republic Army, and it was discovered that the creature was nearly-indestructible.[[33]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast-33) In the hopes of replicating the indestructibility for use in [clone trooper](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper") [armor](/wiki/Clone_trooper_armor "Clone trooper armor"), Chancellor Palpatine approved the creature's relocation to [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant"), the [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") of the Republic. The Zillo Beast escaped from captivity and made its way towards the [Senate Office Building](/wiki/Imperial_Executive_Building "Imperial Executive Building") to find the chancellor, who had ordered the beast be destroyed so its indestructible scales could be removed for testing and replication. The creature [attacked](/wiki/Zillo_Beast_incident "Zillo Beast incident") the Senate Office Building, and Mothma was present during the attack, walking the corridors of power with Senator Organa. The Republic and the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") soon eliminated the creature, bringing an end to the threat against the Senate.[[34]](#cite_note-The_Zillo_Beast_Strikes_Back-34)

 [![Mothma watches the full recording of Deputy Minister Jerec, who argued against a Republic occupation of Mandalore.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/Monmoth.png/revision/latest?cb=20120907214023) [![Mothma watches the full recording of Deputy Minister Jerec, who argued against a Republic occupation of Mandalore.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/Monmoth.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20120907214023)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/Monmoth.png/revision/latest?cb=20120907214023) 

Mothma watches the full recording of Deputy Minister Jerec, who argued against a Republic occupation of Mandalore.

 

The neutrality of the planet [Mandalore](/wiki/Mandalore "Mandalore"), led by [Duchess](/wiki/Duchess "Duchess") [Satine Kryze](/wiki/Satine_Kryze "Satine Kryze"), soon came into dispute when the Mandalorian splinter group known as [Death Watch](/wiki/Death_Watch "Death Watch") threatened to overthrow the pacifist [New Mandalorian](/wiki/New_Mandalorians "New Mandalorians") government that the duchess led. The Senate debated whether or not to send military assistance to Mandalore, a move that the duchess strongly opposed—and one that the Separatists hoped the Republic would enact, as they believed that the people of Mandalore would greet the Death Watch as liberators fighting against a Republic occupation force. The Senate initially voted to send an occupation force, based on doctored evidence suggesting that Mandalore's [Deputy Minister](/wiki/Deputy_Minister "Deputy Minister") [Jerec](/wiki/Jerec "Jerec") called for a Republic presence on his world to combat Death Watch. In actuality, the full recording of Jerec showed that he argued strongly against a military occupation. Mothma was present in the Senate session in which Jerec's true words were broadcast, and the Senate ultimately voted against sending Republic forces to Mandalore.[[35]](#cite_note-Duchess_of_Mandalore-35)

In response to the growing number of refugees displaced by the ongoing war with the Separatists, Amidala and Organa led a [conference](/wiki/Alderaan_Refugee_Conference "Alderaan Refugee Conference") to discuss and, hopefully, resolve the issue. The conference took place on the planet Alderaan, and Mothma was in attendance. She and Organa greeted Amidala, the keynote speaker, when she arrived on Alderaan and escorted her to her quarters. The conference was briefly disrupted when a [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter"), [Aurra Sing](/wiki/Aurra_Sing "Aurra Sing"), attempted to assassinate Amidala on behalf of the [imprisoned](/wiki/Prison "Prison") [crime lord](/wiki/Crime_lord "Crime lord") [Ziro](/wiki/Ziro_Desilijic_Tiure "Ziro Desilijic Tiure") the [Hutt](/wiki/Hutt "Hutt"), but the conference continued onward when Amidala was saved by [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano").[[36]](#cite_note-Assassin-36) Soon after, Senator Mothma attended a party thrown by Amidala in Amidala's apartment in honor of Senator [Aang](/wiki/Aang "Aang"), a member of the [Military Oversight Committee](/wiki/Military_Oversight_Committee "Military Oversight Committee") who was persuaded to vote in favor of reducing military spending.[[37]](#cite_note-Evil_Plans-37)

#### Military funding debate[]

:   "*My dear, you were brilliant.*"  
    "*Thank you, but perhaps we should wait until we actually win the vote before we make a victory speech.*"
:   ―Mon Mothma and Padmé Amidala, following the latter's speech arguing against increased military spending[[38]](#cite_note-Senate_Murders-38)

 [![Senators like Mothma, Amidala, and Onaconda Farr were outspoken opponents of increased military spending.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/AToast-SM.png/revision/latest?cb=20120909063307) [![Senators like Mothma, Amidala, and Onaconda Farr were outspoken opponents of increased military spending.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/AToast-SM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20120909063307)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/34/AToast-SM.png/revision/latest?cb=20120909063307) 

Senators like Mothma, Amidala, and Onaconda Farr were outspoken opponents of increased military spending.

 

The Galactic Senate became embroiled in debates regarding the cost of fighting the Clone Wars. A particularly passionate topic of debate was whether the Senate should fund the creation of more clone troopers to combat the Separatist Alliance, despite the Republic nearing bankruptcy as a result of the war. Senator [Gume Saam](/wiki/Gume_Saam "Gume Saam") argued in favor of a bill that would open new lines of credit to fund the Republic's war effort. Mothma spoke out against the measure, arguing that it would essentially deregulate the banks. The Senate, at Organa's urging, tabled any decision on the proposal until the matter could be considered further. After an [attack](/wiki/Bombing_of_Coruscant%27s_central_power_distribution_grid "Bombing of Coruscant's central power distribution grid") by Separatist [demolition droids](/wiki/Infiltrator_demolition_droid "Infiltrator demolition droid") destroyed Coruscant's [central power distribution grid](/wiki/Central_power_distribution_grid "Central power distribution grid"), the Senate voted on the measure and opted to deregulate the banks in order to open additional lines of credit to fund the war effort.[[39]](#cite_note-Heroes_on_Both_Sides-39)

Despite the passage of the bank deregulation, the debate over increased military funding continued. Senator [Halle Burtoni](/wiki/Halle_Burtoni "Halle Burtoni") of [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino"), the source of the clone troopers, proposed legislation to create five million additional clone soldiers. Organa intended to speak before the Senate in opposition to the bill, but he was injured in an attack by Separatist-aligned bounty hunters [Chata Hyoki](/wiki/Chata_Hyoki "Chata Hyoki") and [Robonino](/wiki/Robonino "Robonino"). As the Senate awaited his address, representatives in favor of Burtoni's bill urged the Senate to vote, while Mothma insisted that the bill's opposition, which included herself, be allowed to speak out against the legislation. With Organa too injured to speak, Amidala addressed the Senate on his behalf, giving an impassioned plea to oppose increased military funding so as to continue funding critical social services for the people of the Republic.[[40]](#cite_note-Pursuit_of_Peace-40)

 [![Senator Onaconda Farr collapses and soon dies after drinking poison, as Mothma and other senators look on.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/Onacondafarrdead.png/revision/latest?cb=20120909030948) [![Senator Onaconda Farr collapses and soon dies after drinking poison, as Mothma and other senators look on.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/Onacondafarrdead.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20120909030948)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/af/Onacondafarrdead.png/revision/latest?cb=20120909030948) 

Senator Onaconda Farr collapses and soon dies after drinking poison, as Mothma and other senators look on.

 

The Senate prepared to vote on the measure, and the bill's opposition continued working to persuade their fellow senators to vote against the increase in military spending. Mothma worked with Amidala, Organa, and Farr in the efforts, and Amidala delivered another speech to the Senate on behalf of their position. The speech was greeted with enthusiasm from the Senate, and Mothma and the other opposition senators celebrated Amidala's address over drinks. Mothma told her former protégé that she did brilliantly, though Amidala was reluctant to feel victorious until such time as Burtoni's bill was struck down. Burtoni herself crashed the conversation, suggesting that the opposition was loyal to the Separatists. Mothma urged the feuding representatives to end their argument, and Farr forced Burtoni to leave the gathering. The senator from Chandrila then praised Farr for leading the efforts against the bill, and the Rodian expressed regret for once siding with the Separatists against the Republic. Mothma assured him, however, that he was now doing the right thing by helping defeat the military spending increase. Farr unexpectedly collapsed after his drink was unknowingly [poisoned](/wiki/Poison "Poison"), so Mothma ran to find help for the dying senator of Rodia. After his death, Mothma attended a memorial service for Farr on a Coruscant landing platform, before the senator's body was returned home.[[38]](#cite_note-Senate_Murders-38)

After the service, Mothma attended a meeting in Chancellor Palpatine's [office](/wiki/Emperor%27s_office "Emperor's office"), where [Lieutenant](/wiki/Lieutenant "Lieutenant") [Tan Divo](/wiki/Tanivos_Exantor_Divo "Tanivos Exantor Divo") of the [Coruscant Security Force](/wiki/Coruscant_Security_Force "Coruscant Security Force") shared his theory that Farr had been murdered. After the meeting, Mothma conversed with Amidala, Organa, and Farr's aide [Lolo Purs](/wiki/Lolo_Purs "Lolo Purs"). Mothma wondered who would have wanted to harm Farr, and, despite Divo's theory that the murder was a result of a secret from Farr's past, Purs speculated that the assassination was the result of Farr's opposition to the spending bill. Organa urged them to put an end to speculation and double their efforts on defeating the bill, but Amidala insisted that they delay the vote until Farr's murderer was apprehended, lest senators vote in favor of the measure in order to avoid harm coming to themselves. Organa agreed to put a delay motion before the Senate while Amidala said she would conduct her own investigation. Mothma questioned her decision, as Divo had asked them not to interfere, but Amidala was sure that they could resolve the case better than Divo, in whom she had little confidence. Organa worried that such an investigation could disrupt the coalition against the bill, a concern that Mothma shared. Knowing that Amidala would see it through anyway, Mothma recommended that Amidala bring her head of security, [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") [Gregar Typho](/wiki/Gregar_Typho "Gregar Typho"), with her, but Amidala preferred to handle it alone. At Mothma's insistence, however, Amidala agreed to work with Senator Organa on her investigation.[[38]](#cite_note-Senate_Murders-38)

During the course of their investigation, Amidala and Organa were targeted for death by the assassin. They were discovered by Lieutenant Divo, who later met with the opposition group, including Mothma, and theorized that the killer was targeting the opposition leadership. Divo placed the group under his protection as he continued the investigation, though Purs left after objecting to having themselves all kept in one room as an easy target. Purs soon returned, claiming she had been attacked by Burtoni, one of the suspects in the murder, which Burtoni laughingly denied. She also denied being involved in the assassination of Senator Farr. Despite suspicion falling onto Burtoni, Amidala realized that Purs had to have been the assassin; the poison targeted Rodians, so Purs would have died too if only she had taken a drink. Her duplicity having been discovered, Purs admitted to killing Farr due to his brief allegiance to the Separatist Alliance, and Purs was arrested for her crime. Soon thereafter, the Senate voted on the funding bill and passed the measure in spite of the opposition efforts of Mothma and the others, leading to the production of more clone troopers.[[38]](#cite_note-Senate_Murders-38)

#### The war continues[]

 [![Mothma, along with Amidala and Organa, attends a peace conference with Separatist representatives on Mandalore.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/15/BecLawiseLetsContinue-AFIN.png/revision/latest?cb=20121211041358) [![Mothma, along with Amidala and Organa, attends a peace conference with Separatist representatives on Mandalore.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/15/BecLawiseLetsContinue-AFIN.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20121211041358)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/15/BecLawiseLetsContinue-AFIN.png/revision/latest?cb=20121211041358) 

Mothma, along with Amidala and Organa, attends a peace conference with Separatist representatives on Mandalore.

 

As the war progressed, a [peace conference](/wiki/Confederate%E2%80%93Republic_peace_conference "Confederate–Republic peace conference") was held between the Republic and the Separatists on the neutral planet of Mandalore, overseen by Duchess Satine. Mothma, Amidala, and Organa represented the Republic in the conference, while three members of the [Separatist Senate](/wiki/Separatist_Senate "Separatist Senate") represented the interests of the Separatist Alliance. The Separatists demanded that the three senators, as representatives for Chancellor Palpatine, recognize the legitimacy of the Separatist Alliance's existence, a stance that the senators were reluctant to take. The talks were disrupted by [Lux Bonteri](/wiki/Lux_Bonteri "Lux Bonteri"), son of the assassinated Separatist Senator [Mina Bonteri](/wiki/Mina_Bonteri "Mina Bonteri"), and asserted that [Count](/wiki/Count "Count") [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku"), the leader of the Separatist Alliance, was behind his mother's death. Bonteri was removed from the talks by [Commando Droid Diplomats](/wiki/Commando_Droid_Diplomat "Commando Droid Diplomat"),[[41]](#cite_note-A_Friend_in_Need-41) but the talks did not result in peace between the two sides.[[32]](#cite_note-Mon_Mothma_Bio_Gallery-32)

The Jedi soon learned that a criminal named [Moralo Eval](/wiki/Moralo_Eval "Moralo Eval") had hatched a plot to kidnap Chancellor Palpatine. In order to infiltrate the conspiracy, led by Count Dooku himself, [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") faked his death so his face could be surgically altered to look like the bounty hunter [Rako Hardeen](/wiki/Rako_Hardeen "Rako Hardeen"), who had fired the shot that supposedly killed the Jedi Master. Believing that Kenobi was dead, Mothma attended the [funeral](/wiki/Funeral_of_Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Funeral of Obi-Wan Kenobi") held for the Jedi Master in the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace").[[42]](#cite_note-Deception-42) Kenobi ultimately disrupted the plot to kidnap the Chancellor, and Palpatine was left unharmed.[[43]](#cite_note-Crisis_on_Naboo-43)

 [![Mothma was one of many dignitaries who attended a funeral for the victims of the Jedi Temple bombing.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/TempleBombingFuneral.png/revision/latest?cb=20131027060205) [![Mothma was one of many dignitaries who attended a funeral for the victims of the Jedi Temple bombing.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/TempleBombingFuneral.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20131027060205)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/TempleBombingFuneral.png/revision/latest?cb=20131027060205) 

Mothma was one of many dignitaries who attended a funeral for the victims of the Jedi Temple bombing.

 

Some time later, Mothma attended yet another funeral in the Jedi Temple, this one for the victims of the [bombing](/wiki/Bombing_of_the_Jedi_Temple_hangar "Bombing of the Jedi Temple hangar") that killed several Jedi and civilians alike.[[44]](#cite_note-The_Jedi_Who_Knew_Too_Much-44) Mothma was a member of the court that would decide the fate of Ahsoka Tano, who was arrested and charged with being the mastermind of the temple attack. Tano was prosecuted by [Admiral](/wiki/Admiral "Admiral") [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin") and defended by Senator Amidala. Ultimately, it was discovered that Jedi Knight [Barriss Offee](/wiki/Barriss_Offee "Barriss Offee"), who had grown disillusioned with the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council") for their leadership in the continuing Clone Wars, was responsible for the plot and had framed her friend and former fellow Padawan for the attack. Tano was freed from Republic custody and chose not to return to the Jedi Order, as she was unwilling to return after the Jedi Council did not trust her innocence.[[45]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-45)

Later in the war, former Senator [Rush Clovis](/wiki/Rush_Clovis "Rush Clovis") was installed as the leader of the [InterGalactic Banking Clan](/wiki/InterGalactic_Banking_Clan "InterGalactic Banking Clan"). He was merely a pawn of Count Dooku, however, and his installation as leader led to a Separatist invasion of [Scipio](/wiki/Scipio "Scipio"), the headquarters of the Banking Clan. The Senate voted to authorize a Republic military strike against the Separatist invasion force, and the Republic was able to repel the Separatists. In response to the actions of the Separatist Alliance, and following the death of Rush Clovis, the Banking Clan senator [Nix Card](/wiki/Nix_Card "Nix Card") ceded control of the banks, [save one branch](/wiki/Muunilinst "Muunilinst"), to Chancellor Palpatine, a move that Mothma reacted to with disapproval. Palpatine promised to reinstate private control of the banks when the Clone Wars were over but urged that it was necessary to ensure financial stability in the interim, a stance that most of the Senate greeted with enthusiastic approval, since the Republic was saved from bankruptcy.[[46]](#cite_note-Crisis_at_the_Heart-46) Shortly thereafter, Mothma was present in a Senate session in which [Queen](/wiki/King "King") [Julia](/wiki/Julia "Julia") of the neutral planet [Bardotta](/wiki/Bardotta "Bardotta") spoke via [hologram](/wiki/Hologram "Hologram") and requested the Republic's assistance in uncovering why Bardottan spiritual leaders were disappearing. At the queen's request, the Republic sent [Gungan](/wiki/Gungan "Gungan") representative [Jar Jar Binks](/wiki/Jar_Jar_Binks "Jar Jar Binks"), as well as Jedi Master [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu"), to help resolve the situation.[[47]](#cite_note-Disappeared_1-47)

#### Ahsoka Tano's trial[]

Mothma was present during the [funeral](/wiki/Funeral_of_the_Jedi_Temple_bombing_victims "Funeral of the Jedi Temple bombing victims") of the six Jedi killed in the [bombing of the Jedi Temple hangar](/wiki/Bombing_of_the_Jedi_Temple_hangar "Bombing of the Jedi Temple hangar"). She also attended the [trial of Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Trial_of_Ahsoka_Tano "Trial of Ahsoka Tano"), who was represented by Amidala, and was seated alongside [Riyo Chuchi](/wiki/Riyo_Chuchi "Riyo Chuchi"), Organa, and [Kin Robb](/wiki/Kin_Robb "Kin Robb") as the former Padawan was accused of masterminding the bombing. Tano was ultimately cleared of all charges when [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") arrived with another Jedi Padwan [Barriss Offee](/wiki/Barriss_Offee "Barriss Offee"), who was the real culprit.[[45]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-45)

Mothma witnessed Offee's confess to her crimes as she explained she, like many others, had come to realize that the Jedi were responsible for the war and they had lost their way becoming the villains in the conflict saying that they should be the ones on trial and that her attack on the Temple was an attack on what the Jedi had become, an army fighting for the dark side, having fallen from the light which they had once held so dear. Offee then stated that the Republic was falling and that it was only a matter of time, before she was pulled back by Skywalker. She was then taken away on the orders of Palpatine.[[45]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-45)

#### Final days of the war[]

:   "*We are loyalists, trying to preserve democracy in the Republic.*"
:   ―Mon Mothma[[48]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars:_Character_Encyclopedia_-_Join_the_Battle!-48)

 [![A meeting of loyalist senators, such as Mothma, planted the seeds of organized rebellion against Palpatine.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/PadmeROTS2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090324192537) [![A meeting of loyalist senators, such as Mothma, planted the seeds of organized rebellion against Palpatine.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/PadmeROTS2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20090324192537)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/PadmeROTS2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090324192537) 

A meeting of loyalist senators, such as Mothma, planted the seeds of organized rebellion against Palpatine.

 

In the final days of the Clone Wars, the Chancellor continued to amass more executive powers. However, in [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"), he was captured by [General](/wiki/General "General") [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous") and taken hostage aboard his ship. As a [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant "Battle of Coruscant") broke out between the Republic and the Confederacy, Skywalker and Kenobi rushed to Palpatine's rescue. They managed to retrieve their kidnapped Chancellor, killing Count Dooku in the process. In the wake of the rescue and subsequent battle, Organa gathered outside the Senate Building with the Loyalist Committee, and they all greeted Palpatine.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_III-12)

Palpatine was soon given control of the Jedi Council, and he soon began appointing regional governors to oversee all [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system") in the Republic. Alarmed by these abrupt chain of events, a small group of concerned senators, such as Organa, Amidala, Mothma, and [Meena Tills](/wiki/Meena_Tills "Meena Tills"), met in Organa's office at [Cantham House](/wiki/Cantham_House "Cantham House").[[23]](#cite_note-Rogue_One_Visual_Dictionary-23) Throughout these events, Mothma and Senator Organa met in secret, even from their allies, to discuss basic plans for an organized and armed rebellion against the possibility that Palpatine may become a tyrant.[[28]](#cite_note-HC_40-28) These meetings eventually set the spark for a highly secret Rebellion movement.[[3]](#cite_note-Character_Encyclopedia-3)

Later, Mothma and the rest of the senators met in [Padmé Amidala's apartment](/wiki/Naboo_Queen_(restaurant) "Naboo Queen (restaurant)"), where Mothma told them that they were forming an alliance to stop Palpatine. However, Padmé suggested bringing the plan to the one Jedi she trusts, but Mothma and the group agreed with Organa to appeal to the Senate first.[[3]](#cite_note-Character_Encyclopedia-3)

 [![Mothma attended the funeral of her dear friend, Padmé Amidala.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6d/OrganaMothmaFuneral-Resolve.png/revision/latest?cb=20221029055934) [![Mothma attended the funeral of her dear friend, Padmé Amidala.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6d/OrganaMothmaFuneral-Resolve.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20221029055934)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6d/OrganaMothmaFuneral-Resolve.png/revision/latest?cb=20221029055934) 

Mothma attended the funeral of her dear friend, Padmé Amidala.

 

The Clone Wars came to a close following the deaths of Count Dooku and the droid [General](/wiki/General "General") [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous"). Skywalker discovered that Palpatine was secretly Darth Sidious, a [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith") who had manipulated the entire conflict to gain power over the Republic. Mace Windu and three other Jedi Masters attempted to arrest the chancellor, but the Dark Lord killed them all and seduced Skywalker to the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force"), anointing him as the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") Darth Vader. Having found justification to eliminate his enemies, Palpatine declared the Jedi Order to be enemies of the Republic and ordered Darth Vader and clone troopers across the galaxy to destroy the Jedi. A disfigured Chancellor, injured in his [confrontation](/wiki/Duel_in_Palpatine%27s_office "Duel in Palpatine's office") with Master Windu, spoke to the Senate about the so-called Jedi betrayal and [proclaimed](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") that, in the interest of stability and security, the Republic would be reorganized into the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"). The worst fears of Mothma and her allies were confirmed, and Amidala died soon thereafter on the asteroid Polis Massa.[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_III-12) Mothma soon met with Bail, and together they attended Padmé's funeral on Theed alongside thousands of others.[[49]](#cite_note-Resolve-49)

During the [senatorial arrests](/wiki/Senatorial_arrests "Senatorial arrests"), Mothma was among the senators charged with colluding with the Jedi Order and treason, yet she, like Bail Organa, was released after publicly claiming to be a loyal Imperial.[[22]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-22) Amidala's death was blamed on the Jedi Rebellion, but Mothma, who attended [her close friend's funeral](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala%27s_funeral "Padmé Amidala's funeral"), knew who was really at fault — Palpatine. Vowing to return democracy to the galaxy,[[50]](#cite_note-Mon_Mothma_card-50) Mothma and Organa continued to prepare for resistance to the [Emperor's](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") rule.[[32]](#cite_note-Mon_Mothma_Bio_Gallery-32)

#### An attempt to restore democracy[]

:   "*I've laid out a framework for what I'm calling the Imperial Rebirth Act. My goal is not to create a public stir or incur the ire of Palpatine's supporters. I will argue this bill clarifies the new division of powers, that it will streamline decision-making and guide future legislation in this bold new era. In reality, the bill is designed to secure the Senate's position and avert executive overreach while allowing Palpatine to save face.*"
:   ―Mon Mothma[[7]](#cite_note-MOF-7)

In 19 BBY,[[51]](#cite_note-MOFDateRebirthAct-51) in order to try to curb Emperor Palpatine's executive power, Mothma drafted the [Imperial Rebirth Act](/wiki/Imperial_Rebirth_Act "Imperial Rebirth Act"). She sought political support for the bill among the members of the Delegation of the 2,000, former Separatists worlds under the leadership of [Tychon Nulvolio](/wiki/Tychon_Nulvolio "Tychon Nulvolio"), and powerful magnates [Arvik Cornade](/wiki/Arvik_Cornade "Arvik Cornade"), [Baron](/wiki/Baron "Baron") [Shkan-Shkan Yew](/wiki/Shkan-Shkan_Yew "Shkan-Shkan Yew"), and [Hasalia Prederiko](/wiki/Hasalia_Prederiko "Hasalia Prederiko"). During that time, Mothma had her apartment broken into by [Thalvus Agyomenidus](/wiki/Thalvus_Agyomenidus "Thalvus Agyomenidus"), a radicalized member of the pro-Imperial activist group [4040s](/wiki/4040s "4040s"), who killed her aide and Imperial spy [Zhuna](/wiki/Zhuna "Zhuna"). Mothma and her husband were relocated to a temporary apartment by [Senate Security](/wiki/Senate_Security "Senate Security"), which also was broken into sometime later.[[7]](#cite_note-MOF-7)

In the context of the Empire's spying on Senator Bail Organa during his [investigation into the framing of the Jedi](/wiki/Investigation_into_the_framing_of_the_Jedi "Investigation into the framing of the Jedi"), Mothma was again imprisoned and interrogated over her association with Organa, and released sometime after.[[7]](#cite_note-MOF-7)

As a precondition for Organa's support for her bill, she agreed to meet up with former Separatist operative [Soujen Vak-Nhalis](/wiki/Soujen_Vak-Nhalis "Soujen Vak-Nhalis") and share his evidence with the Senate of the falsification of records that were used as justification for branding the Jedi traitors. Mothma and Vak-Nhalis, whose true plan was to [kill the Emperor](/wiki/Attack_on_the_Executive_Center "Attack on the Executive Center"), headed to the [Imperial Executive Building](/wiki/Imperial_Executive_Building "Imperial Executive Building"). Mothma had previously learned from Nulvolio that, amidst the modifications Vak-Nhalis underwent, a self-destruction mechanism was also added, triggered by the sound of the words "oubliette" and "sublime." Fearing that Vak-Nhalis's attempt on Palpatine's life would make it politically impossible to pass her bill, she activated the detonation, killing Vak-Nhalis and wounding herself in the process.[[7]](#cite_note-MOF-7)

In the aftermath of the explosion, Mothma spent over a week at a [medcenter](/wiki/Medcenter "Medcenter") in recovery, during which the Imperial Rebirth Act passed in the Senate. Sometime thereafter, Grand Vizier Mas Amedda met with Mothma, and revealed that Palpatine was to veto provisions of her bill that limited the Emperor's powers, citing his [century plan](/wiki/Century_plan "Century plan") for the galaxy. Amedda took her to see to the reeducation camp [Center One](/wiki/Center_One "Center One"), where political prisoners were jailed, in an attempt to keep Mothma in line.[[7]](#cite_note-MOF-7)

Mothma continued serving in the Senate by [7 BBY](/wiki/7_BBY "7 BBY"), where she and Senator Organa spent a lot of time pleading with their fellow senators to recognize the state of the Empire, but their speeches were dismissed without further consideration.[[52]](#cite_note-RebelRising-52)

### The Rebel Alliance[]

#### Rebellion from within[]

:   "*Don't lecture me on vulnerability. No one's more at risk than I am. You think I haven't thought this through? I'd be the first one to fall.*"
:   ―Mothma to Luthen Rael, on their rebel practices[[53]](#cite_note-Aldhani-53)

 [![Senator Mothma in the Imperial Senate](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e0/Imperial_Senator_Mothma-Andor.png/revision/latest?cb=20220802120722) [![Senator Mothma in the Imperial Senate](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e0/Imperial_Senator_Mothma-Andor.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20220802120722)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e0/Imperial_Senator_Mothma-Andor.png/revision/latest?cb=20220802120722) 

Senator Mothma in the Imperial Senate

 

Though Mothma and Organa remained members of the [Imperial Senate](/wiki/Imperial_Senate "Imperial Senate"), they understood that the political group was now irrelevant, and that the time came for rebellion. While Organa dealt with the military aspects of building a rebellion and grew its network of intelligence agents, Mothma further developed political alliances that were made during the final moments of the Republic. Mothma understood that those alliances would be key for any future galactic governance after either the defeat or the reform of the Empire.[[28]](#cite_note-HC_40-28) Before Amidala died, she secretly gave [birth](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") to [twins](/wiki/Twin "Twin"): [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker") and [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo"), the latter of whom was adopted by Organa and his wife, Queen [Breha Organa](/wiki/Breha_Organa "Breha Organa").[[12]](#cite_note-Episode_III-12) Mothma knew the adopted [Princess](/wiki/Princess "Princess") from an early age and watched as she grew to become a politician in her own right. Mothma became the princess' political tutor, teaching her before she took her father's place in the [Imperial Senate](/wiki/Imperial_Senate "Imperial Senate"), and watched as the princess became a leader in the emerging rebellion against the Empire.[[20]](#cite_note-Moving_Target-20)

Around [18 BBY](/wiki/18_BBY "18 BBY"),[[54]](#cite_note-18_BBY_Date-54) Mothma and Perrin had a child, a daughter named [Leida Mothma](/wiki/Leida_Mothma "Leida Mothma").[[11]](#cite_note-Databank_Leida-11) Mon and Leida had a distant relationship, with Mon also hiding her rebellious activities from her daughter[[55]](#cite_note-Space_Moms-55) and husband.[[16]](#cite_note-Announcement-16) While there were times she wanted to tell Leida about the hidden part of her career, Mon decided that keeping Leida out of the loop kept her safe.[[55]](#cite_note-Space_Moms-55)

While continuing her work in the Imperial Senate, Mothma continued to expand on the loose network of rebel cells she began calling "the Alliance." These groups included organizations such as the [Atrivis Resistance Group](/wiki/Atrivis_Resistance_Group "Atrivis Resistance Group"), which joined Mothma's network in 5 BBY.[[22]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-22) In [5 BBY](/wiki/5_BBY "5 BBY"),[[56]](#cite_note-AndorDate-56) Mothma visited [Luthen Rael](/wiki/Luthen_Rael "Luthen Rael")'s [Galactic Antiquities and Objects of Interest](/wiki/Galactic_Antiquities_and_Objects_of_Interest "Galactic Antiquities and Objects of Interest") on Coruscant, claiming to buy a present for her husband for his [Day of Days](/wiki/Day_of_Days "Day of Days"). In reality, however, Mothma had come to speak with Rael, whom she was trying to smuggle [money](/wiki/Galactic_Credit_Standard "Galactic Credit Standard") to in order to feed the [rebel network](/wiki/Axis_network "Axis network") he was running. By this time, the Empire had begun sending spies after Mothma, including her new driver, [Kloris](/wiki/Exmar_Kloris "Exmar Kloris"), meaning she was unable to transfer the money. Upon her arrival, Rael led the senator to the back of the gallery, feigning to show her military artifacts her husband would enjoy. She told Rael that she was looking to lean Perrin's interest from ancient weapons, to other objects. He then brought her to the back to show her other items. Once in the back, Mothma informed Rael that she had found someone who they could bring into their circle, but Luthen dismissed this as they were vulnerable enough. Mothma, however, told him not to lecture her on vulnerability, as if they were discovered, she would be the first to fall. Mothma then left the gallery and quietly observed Coruscant on her way [home](/wiki/Chandrilan_Embassy "Chandrilan Embassy").[[53]](#cite_note-Aldhani-53)

#### Familial and senatorial challenges[]

:   "*Oh, are they? Are they fun? We should find some Ghorman guests for tonight and see how amused they are. Your fun friends just cut off their shipping lanes yesterday. Do you know how many will starve? Oh, perhaps we can laugh about it over the third course.*"
:   ―Mothma to Perrin, on Perrin's suggestions for their party's guest list[[53]](#cite_note-Aldhani-53)

When Mothma returned to her apartment, she found Fertha preparing for a dinner party for his regimental friend, the [governor](/wiki/Governor "Governor") of Hanna, about which he had told his wife about a [month](/wiki/Standard_month "Standard month") prior. Mothma asked who else Fertha had invited, and was upset to learn that he had invited several of her political enemies, including [Ars Dangor](/wiki/Ars_Dangor "Ars Dangor") and [Sly Moore](/wiki/Sly_Moore "Sly Moore"), who, the day before, had cut off the [Ghorman](/wiki/Ghorman "Ghorman") [shipping lanes](/wiki/Hyperspace_route "Hyperspace route"). Mothma protested that she be seated away from them, with Perrin asserting that she would be seated at the "boring side of the table." Annoyed and frustrated, Mothma stormed away.[[53]](#cite_note-Aldhani-53)

 [![Mothma's daughter Leida Mothma](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f0/Leida-Andor5.png/revision/latest?cb=20221012042743) [![Mothma's daughter Leida Mothma](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f0/Leida-Andor5.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20221012042743)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f0/Leida-Andor5.png/revision/latest?cb=20221012042743) 

Mothma's daughter Leida Mothma

 

The next morning, Mothma had breakfast with Fertha and the[[57]](#cite_note-The_Axe_Forgets-57) thirteen-year-old[[58]](#cite_note-Leida_Databank-58) Leida. At the last minute, Leida cancelled plans she had had with her mother to take Leida to her classes, asking her father to take her instead. The two then got into an argument as Leida claimed that Mothma only took her to show off that she was involved somehow. When Mothma told her how hurtful that was, Leida said that it just proved her point that everything was all about Mothma. Fertha remained mostly silent during the exchange. Mothma then sarcastically thanked her husband for his help in the disagreement.[[57]](#cite_note-The_Axe_Forgets-57)

Later that night, Mothma and Fertha attended an event together. On the way back in a speeder, driven by Kloris, Fertha mentioned how Mothma had watched his conversation with [Gar Tafeed](/wiki/Gar_Tafeed "Gar Tafeed") whom he claimed knew more about what she was up to than he did. He also asked Mothma why he had not made mention of her [new foundation](/wiki/Chandrilan_charitable_outreach_program "Chandrilan charitable outreach program"), to which Mothma responded that she assumed that Fertha would not be interested as it was charitable. Fertha then asked Mothma, for the second time that day, for their driver's name which she told him was Kloris before he asked him to take the [Expressway](/wiki/Expressway "Expressway").[[57]](#cite_note-The_Axe_Forgets-57)

The next day, Mothma appeared before the Imperial Senate, although the senate chamber was almost empty. Mothma showed her support for Senator [Dhow](/wiki/Dhow "Dhow")'s proposal, calling it both temperate and timely, and putting in place a fact-finding commission for the session that would prove that the opposition to Dhow's proposal would cause further harm to the [Ghormans](/wiki/Ghorman_(people) "Ghorman (people)"). Mothma attempted to pass her own bill which would also provide aid to the Ghormans. Mothma was disappointed however to see that most of the Senate weren't paying attention to her with many looking at their datapads before exiting their pods. She then picked up her own datapad, as an alarm had gone off, as news broke on Coruscant about how rebels had stolen eighty million credits on [Aldhani](/wiki/Aldhani "Aldhani").[[59]](#cite_note-The_Eye-59)

#### A delicate conversation with an old friend[]

:   "*What you see, what people say about me, it's a clear picture, isn't it. I'm a polite, sometimes-indecisive Senator who spends her days fighting and failing to protect Separatist do-gooders and battle Empire overreach. An irritation, as you so harshly put it.*"  
    "*I've made you angry, I…*"  
    "*No, No. You've set me free. I've been wondering all day how I could be sure of confiding in you.*"  
    "*I don't know what we're talking about.*"  
    "*It's a lie. The Mon Mothma people think they know, it's a lie. It's a projection. It's a front. Smile. I've learned from Palpatine. I show you the stone in my hand, you miss the knife at your throat.*"
:   ―Mon Mothma and Tay Kolma[[16]](#cite_note-Announcement-16)

Shortly after Mothma returned to Rael's store claiming that she wanted to switch out Fertha's gift for another one, though in reality she wanted to confront Rael about the [attack on Aldhani](/wiki/Aldhani_heist "Aldhani heist"). Rael claimed that he needed credits which Mothma could no longer give, but Mothma was angered by Rael's actions as it would lead to more suffering as the Empire would crack down on other planets. Rael expected this, but saw the suffering of others, due to the Empire's paranoia, as necessary to defeating the Empire. Mothma then said she would not be taking either of the items and left to return to her vehicle.[[16]](#cite_note-Announcement-16)

 [![At a party, hosted at her apartment, Mothma asked her old friend Tay Kolma for help](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/TayKolma.png/revision/latest?cb=20220801163445) [![At a party, hosted at her apartment, Mothma asked her old friend Tay Kolma for help](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/TayKolma.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20220801163445)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/TayKolma.png/revision/latest?cb=20220801163445) 

At a party, hosted at her apartment, Mothma asked her old friend Tay Kolma for help

 

Later that night, Mothma hosted a party at her apartment, where she talked with her school friend, the [banker](/wiki/Bank "Bank") [Tay Kolma](/wiki/Tay_Kolma "Tay Kolma"). Mothma reintroduced Kolma to Leida, whom he had met when she was young. Leida did not remember, however, and mostly ignored Kolma as she asked her mother's permission to be excused from the party like Fertha had told her to do. After Leida left, Mothma inquired if she could ask Kolma for a political favor, but Kolma advised against it, warning that his political opinions were getting stronger as he had been continually growing less and less fond of the Empire. Kolma did not approve of Mothma spending so much time with those inside the Empire and how interlinked she had become with the Empire.[[16]](#cite_note-Announcement-16)

Mothma then took Kolma aside into the living room to tell him that her image of a deferential Senator who continually fails to achieve her goals of opposing Empire overreach was a lie. Mothma revealed to Kolma that the [Grand Vizier](/wiki/Grand_Vizier "Grand Vizier") had infiltrated her Separatist Coalition meetings and her driver was a member of the [Imperial Security Bureau](/wiki/Imperial_Security_Bureau "Imperial Security Bureau") who reported on her secret humanitarian programs. She wanted the Empire to watch her because if everyone thought of her as an "irritation," that meant there was a good chance they would miss what she was really doing. Kolma then asked what Mothma was "really doing" to which Mothma responded that she was raising money and that she could no longer freely access her family accounts. Kolma asked what she was raising money for, but Mothma ignored him and said that she was was forming a Chandrilan charitable outreach program of which she would ask Kolma to be the [chairman](/wiki/Chairman "Chairman"), which would involve a lot of trips to Coruscant and would appear to be another of her benevolent and bothersome actions. When Kolma pointed out that she hadn't answered his question, Mothma told him that she would not as he was better off not knowing.[[16]](#cite_note-Announcement-16)

The pair were then interrupted by Fertha who assumed that they were reminiscing about their school days and reminded the pair of an upcoming reunion. Mothma then left the living room with Fertha to talk to some of the other guests.[[16]](#cite_note-Announcement-16)

#### Opposition to authoritarian measures[]

:   "*In the Imperial Senate a common joke about Mon Mothma, as she would later recount, was that she was obsessed with trying to save the Empire from the Emperor.*"
:   ―Beaumont Kin, *The Rise and Fall of the Galactic Empire*[[60]](#cite_note-RiseFall-60)

Mothma was a prominent opponent of the new authoritarian laws that Emperor Palpatine introduced to the Imperial Senate following a [rebel attack in Aldhani](/wiki/Aldhani_heist "Aldhani heist"),[[10]](#cite_note-Narkina_5-10) specifically the [Imperial Emergency Act](/wiki/Imperial_Emergency_Act "Imperial Emergency Act") and the [Public Order Resentencing Directive](/wiki/Public_Order_Resentencing_Directive "Public Order Resentencing Directive").[[24]](#cite_note-Nobody's_Listening-24) Mothma hosted a banquet on Coruscant with the ulterior motive of attempting to muster enough votes to stop the legislation, deciding to present the argument of saving the Empire from the Emperor. Once Fertha left Mothma's side, Kolma, who was attending the party, warned Mothma that the Empire's new banking laws would hinder their operations. After speaking with many senators and giving a speech about how young she and Fertha were when they came to Coruscant, Fertha revealed that Kolma left early.[[10]](#cite_note-Narkina_5-10)

Mothma was particularly critical of the PORD legislation, which she voiced opposition to in the Senate and called "the next step of an all too predictable march toward complete unchallenged authority". Her opposition raised a certain amount of debate, but the acts were eventually passed nonetheless. Later that day, Mothma's cousin Vel Sartha arrived at the embassy with a dress as a gift for Leida. While Mothma pressed Sartha to figure out why she had been gone for so long, Sartha kept her activities vague and avoided discussing Rael's activities by reminding Mothma of their vow of secrecy.[[24]](#cite_note-Nobody's_Listening-24) Unbeknownst to Mothma, Sartha had been one of the rebels who performed the heist on Aldhani.[[59]](#cite_note-The_Eye-59) The next day, Mothma encouraged Sartha to keep playing of the part of spoiled rich girl to hide her true actions before Sartha left for Chandrila.[[24]](#cite_note-Nobody's_Listening-24)

#### Financing Rebellion[]

Kolma approached Mothma with concerns that the large sums of money Mothma was moving would be noticed by the Empire soon. Deciding that she needed a loan, Kolma suggested going to wealthy criminal banker [Davo Sculdun](/wiki/Davo_Sculdun "Davo Sculdun") for help. Kolma noted that Sculdun would not concern himself with what Mothma was doing with her money, but Mothma was still hesitant to work with Sculdun.[[24]](#cite_note-Nobody's_Listening-24) Eventually, Kolma arranged a meeting between him, Mothma, and Sculdun. Sculdun offered solutions to make Mothma's transactions harder to detect by increased Imperial scrutiny, and initially indicated that he would do it for free. However, Sculdun revealed that his price was an introduction between his son [Stekan Sculdun](/wiki/Stekan_Sculdun "Stekan Sculdun") and Leida, suggesting the Chandrilan betrothal tradition that Mothma had taken part in as a teenager and thus resented. When Sculdun confirmed that was his only offer, Mothma said she would not consider it, but Sculdun stated that he knew she was lying and was actually considering it.[[61]](#cite_note-One_Way_Out-61)

Later, Mothma and Sartha watched Leida participate in a traditional Chandrilan courtship ritual involving other young girls and an elder, that Leida had decided to participate in of her own volition, both realizing that Leida is actually supportive of traditions that they consider archaic. While they watch, Mothma explained her financial situation to Sartha, including her plans with Kolma that were jeopardized by the missing credits on her ledger. She revealed that she had kept the extent of the situation hidden from Rael, but suggested she may have found a solution.[[62]](#cite_note-Daughter_of_Ferrix-62)

Mothma's desperation to avoid her rebel activities from being exposed via her banking records[[62]](#cite_note-Daughter_of_Ferrix-62) led to her agreeing to [Davo Sculdun](/wiki/Davo_Sculdun "Davo Sculdun")'s proposal.[[63]](#cite_note-Rix_Road-63) Mothma introduced Leida to his son, [Stekan Sculdun](/wiki/Stekan_Sculdun "Stekan Sculdun"), putting both on the road to an arranged marriage.[[61]](#cite_note-One_Way_Out-61)

#### Leia's Day of Demand[]

:   "*There comes a time when refusing to stop violence can no longer be called nonviolence. We cease to be objectors and become bystanders. At some point, morality must be wedded to action, or else it's no more than mere...vanity.* "
:   ―Senator Mon Mothma[[64]](#cite_note-Leia_Princess_of_Alderaan-64)

 [![Mothma helped Leia Organa during her time as an Apprentice Legislator](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/76/ApprenticeLegislator-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190728020838) [![Mothma helped Leia Organa during her time as an Apprentice Legislator](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/76/ApprenticeLegislator-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20190728020838)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/76/ApprenticeLegislator-LeiaManga.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190728020838) 

Mothma helped Leia Organa during her time as an Apprentice Legislator

 

In [3 BBY](/wiki/3_BBY "3 BBY"),[[65]](#cite_note-LPOA_Date-65) Mothma attended [Leia Organa's Day of Demand](/wiki/Leia_Organa%27s_Day_of_Demand "Leia Organa's Day of Demand") at the [Royal Palace of Alderaan](/wiki/Royal_Palace_of_Alderaan "Royal Palace of Alderaan"), where she smiled wider as Leia passed, along with several dinner parties hosted at the palace which actually served as strategy meetings for the growing rebellion. By that time, with Mothma serving as the [Senior Senator](/wiki/Senior_Senator "Senior Senator") of Chandrila, she was joined in her Chandrilian delegation of the Senate by Senator [Winmey Lenz](/wiki/Winmey_Lenz "Winmey Lenz").[[64]](#cite_note-Leia_Princess_of_Alderaan-64)

Before one of these dinner parties, Mothma talked with Princess Leia about her time in the [Apprentice Legislature](/wiki/Apprentice_Legislature "Apprentice Legislature"). Leia confessed her guilt to Mothma about falling for a trick planted by the Empire as she had recommended [Arreyel](/wiki/Arreyel "Arreyel") to be chosen for the location of a new [Imperial Academy](/wiki/Imperial_Academy "Imperial Academy") which allowed the Empire to run scans that showed the existence of a powerful radiation source under under the planet's crust. The Empire then began plans to use the source in planet-wide factories and gave the population six weeks to evacuate with no compensation. Mothma reassured Leia that Palpatine and his higher ups were skilled at those things and that even she herself had fallen for them a few times. Mothma moved into the banquet hall for the dinner party, shortly after, where they discussed the recent [assassination](/wiki/Strike_on_Onoam "Strike on Onoam") of [Moff](/wiki/Moff "Moff") [Panaka](/wiki/Quarsh_Panaka "Quarsh Panaka") and the idea of implementing further violence into their plans. Mothma pointed out that at some point refusing to fight stopped being nonviolence and instead of being objectors they became bystanders. Like Breha Organa, Mothma tried to get Bail to recognize that a large scale military rebellion was the only way to rife the galaxy of Palpatine and the Empire.[[64]](#cite_note-Leia_Princess_of_Alderaan-64)

The next day, Leia visited Mothma in her [office](/wiki/Mon_Mothma%27s_Senate_office "Mon Mothma's Senate office") with proof of the Empire's actions towards the planet [Chasmeene](/wiki/Chasmeene "Chasmeene"), having punished them for failing to meet the Imperial quota by irradiation of vast swaths of its farmland, which led to planet wide famine. Mothma told Leia that there was very little that could be done with the evidence that she'd gathered. Mothma explained to Leia that worlds such as Chasmeene weren't subject to as much propaganda and that it wasn't ignorance, but rather tyranny and fear, that kept worlds within the Empire. Mothma did reassure Leia, however, that evidence, such as the one she gathered, would be useful for when Palpatine fell and they would need to "rewrite their false history to reflect the truth". Mothma also told Leia that she was honoured that Leia had trusted her with this as the Empire had worked hard to destroy peoples faith in each other and that it was only by reaching out that they would be able to make the allies they needed. When Leia hoped that one day she would be one of those allies, Mothma reassured her that she already was.[[64]](#cite_note-Leia_Princess_of_Alderaan-64)

At another one of the dinner parties, [Grand Moff](/wiki/Grand_Moff "Grand Moff") Tarkin unexpectedly attended and in order to hide the true purpose of the gathering Queen Breha pretended to drunkenly accuse her husband and Mothma of having an affair resulting in Princess Leia bursting into tears and Tarkin stomping out. The Organas' allies then realized that Leia was aware of their dangerous and illegal activities and were greatly angered that Bail and Breha had allowed their child to know about it. Mothma then told everyone that Leia Organa wasn't a child as she had had her [Day of Demand](/wiki/Day_of_Demand "Day of Demand") and was on the verge of becoming an adult. Mothma said that Leia was growing into a "representative of the next generation", a generation she said would do most of the fighting and dying in what was to come.[[64]](#cite_note-Leia_Princess_of_Alderaan-64)

Later, Mothma attended the [ceremony](/wiki/Coronation_of_the_Alderaanian_heir "Coronation of the Alderaanian heir") where Leia was officially invested as [crown](/wiki/Crown "Crown") princess of Alderaan.[[64]](#cite_note-Leia_Princess_of_Alderaan-64) The young Organa would go onto join the Imperial Senate. Like Leia, Mothma would support a refugee rights bill in the Senate that kept refugees safe from exploitation. After it passed, it cost a chief operating officer on Coruscant billions, which eventually led to her putting a bounty out on both Mothma and Leia.[[66]](#cite_note-The_Princess_and_the_Scoundrel-66)

#### Resigning for the Rebellion[]

##### Final speech in the Senate[]

:   "*Here we are. This day has finally come.*"  
    "*You don't have to do this.*"  
    "*If you're brave enough to stay, I should be brave enough to go.*"
:   ―Mon Mothma and Bail Organa, before the former's address to the senate and escape[[21]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_the_Rebellion-21)

 [![Ghorman senator Dasi Oran is arrested.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/Welcome-SenatorialArrest.png/revision/latest?cb=20250510040035) [![Ghorman senator Dasi Oran is arrested.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/Welcome-SenatorialArrest.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250510040035)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8d/Welcome-SenatorialArrest.png/revision/latest?cb=20250510040035) 

Ghorman senator Dasi Oran is arrested.

 

Following the [Ghorman Massacre](/wiki/Ghorman_Massacre "Ghorman Massacre") in 2 BBY, Senator [Dasi Oran](/wiki/Dasi_Oran "Dasi Oran") was arrested without a warrant or charges levied against him in the Senate Building, in front of a wide range of senators, including Mothma and Bail Organa. Following the arrest, Mothma appealed to Organa's significant power and seniority in the senate with the hope that she could be included in the next session's order of business. The scale of the misinformation campaign against the Ghorman people had reached extreme levels, but Mon asserted that the lies were obvious and felt it was important to speak up even when the Empire's significant control over the senate meant that it would be hard for her to get time on the floor. However, she and Organa both agreed the speech would be potent enough to cause retaliation, and based the decision to speak upon the idea that Mon would flee Coruscant and forfeit her position as senator immediately thereafter. Organa informed her that he would organise a team to extract her, but that he would stay within the senate for a longer period as to keep the Empire's anxieties at bay.[[21]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_the_Rebellion-21)

Following this discussion, Mon spent a whole night in the senate writing and preparing her speech, but also checking, with the help of [Erskin Semaj](/wiki/Erskin_Semaj "Erskin Semaj") - her senatorial attaché, for listening devices in her office following Organa's assertion that [Senator Ton](/wiki/Ton "Ton") had found a listening device in her own. Upon its discovery, she destroyed it, provoking the interests of ISB agents. Under the incorrect impression that more listening devices may exist, she left her office to practice her speech in a plaza of the Senate, where she was approached by Luthen Rael, who revealed Semaj was one of his agents and had been since the wedding of Mon's daughter, Leida. Luthen also revealed that there was a mole within the extraction team provided by Bail Organa, information he was given by ISB Supervisor [Lonni Jung](/wiki/Lonni_Jung "Lonni Jung"). He offered an alternative solution to Organa's team: extraction by Cassian Andor using the code phrase 'I have friends everywhere'.[[21]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_the_Rebellion-21) This meeting was the final time that the two would encounter.[[67]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Luthen_and_Mon-67)

 [![Mothma delivers her speech to the Senate.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/WelcometotheRebellion-EpisodeThumbnail.png/revision/latest?cb=20250507043435) [![Mothma delivers her speech to the Senate.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/WelcometotheRebellion-EpisodeThumbnail.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20250507043435)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b5/WelcometotheRebellion-EpisodeThumbnail.png/revision/latest?cb=20250507043435) 

Mothma delivers her speech to the Senate.

 

The following day the senate session started with the ISB, senators, and the press under the impression that Mothma would not be speaking - [ISB Supervisor Lagret](/wiki/Lagret "Lagret") informed one of his officers that he had received the senate's agenda and Mon was not on it.
