However, Senator [Erveen](/wiki/Erveen "Erveen"), the senator from [Hodi](/wiki/Hodi "Hodi") and a respected figure as well as a close ally of Bail Organa's, was on the agenda, and she chose to yield some of her time to Organa due to an 'important point of order'. Organa then invoked [Article 17-252](/wiki/Article_17-252 "Article 17-252"), a piece of legislation proposed by the [Emperor's Council](/wiki/Imperial_Ruling_Council "Imperial Ruling Council") directly that "a senior senator, in the case of emergency, may yield the floor freely without interruption to another senior senator." Given that all three - Erveen, Organa, and Mothma, were all senior senators, they were free to yield this time, and as article 17-252 was in effect the speaker did not have the power to override Mothma's speech. The ISB, however, did attempt to shut down the public broadcast of Mothma's speech.[[21]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_the_Rebellion-21)

|  |
| --- |
| **Attribution**: Mon Mothma gives her final address to the Imperial Senate |
| Fellow senators, friends, colleagues… allies, adversaries… I stand before you this morning with a heavy heart. I've spent my life in this chamber. I came here as a child… and as I look around me now, I realize that I have almost no memories that predate my arrival, and few bonds that cleave so tightly. Through these many years, I believe I have served my constituents honorably and upheld our code of conduct. This chamber is a cauldron of opinions, and we've certainly all had our patience and tempers tested in our pursuit of our ideals. Disagree as we might, I am hopeful that those of you who know me will vouch for my credibility in the days to come. I stand this morning with a difficult message. I believe we are in crisis. The distance between what is said and what is known to be true has become an abyss. Of all the things at risk, the loss of an objective reality is perhaps the most dangerous. The death of truth is the ultimate victory of evil. When truth leaves us, when we let it slip away, when it is ripped from our hands, we become vulnerable to the appetite of whatever monster screams the loudest. This chamber's hold on the truth was finally lost on the Ghorman Plaza. What took place yesterday… what happened yesterday on Ghorman was unprovoked genocide. Yes, genocide! And that truth has been exiled from this chamber! And the monster screaming the loudest? The monster we've helped create? The monster who will come for us all soon enough… is Emperor Palpatine! | |

The speech, aimed at both elected officials in the Senate and the galaxy's diverse inhabitants,[[68]](#cite_note-) was met with loud jeering and rejection on the Senate floor, as well as the end of the current session due to the shutdown of the public broadcast.[[21]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_the_Rebellion-21)

##### Escaping the Empire[]

:   "*I name the Emperor himself for ordering the brutal attacks on the people of Ghorman. Their peaceful world is one of countless systems helpless against his oppressive rule. This massacre is proof that our self-appointed Emperor is little more than a lying executioner, imposing his tyranny under the pretense of security. We cannot allow this evil to stand.*"
:   ―Mon Mothma's transmission to the galaxy after fleeing the Senate[[69]](#cite_note-Secret_Cargo-69)

 [![An ISB agent attempts to arrest Mothma as she tries to leave the Senate building.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/Andor-EscapeFromTheSenate.png/revision/latest?cb=20250508122713) [![An ISB agent attempts to arrest Mothma as she tries to leave the Senate building.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/Andor-EscapeFromTheSenate.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20250508122713)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/08/Andor-EscapeFromTheSenate.png/revision/latest?cb=20250508122713) 

An ISB agent attempts to arrest Mothma as she tries to leave the Senate building.

 

Immediately following the speech, ISB forces ordered her arrest and that authorities prevent her from leaving the senate building. With her driver an ISB double agent, her office was raided and the building was shut down with the ISB believing she would not use deadly force to escape. Meanwhile, she met Cassian Andor, who communicated his identity through the code phrase 'I have friends everywhere' as well as revealing to Mon that he and Mon's cousin, Vel, were the last survivors of the [heist on Aldhani](/wiki/Aldhani_heist "Aldhani heist"). They headed at first towards the loading bay, where Luthen and Kleya were waiting with a ship, but after the ISB agent managed by Lonni Jung in Organa's extraction team tried to intervene and arrest Mothma, the Imperial Navy had time to lock down that part of the building. Instead, Mothma lead Andor back to her parked private car, where Andor killed the vehicle's driver - ISB-paid Kloris - taking control of the vehicle and escaping to a [safehouse of Luthen's](/wiki/Axis_network_safehouse "Axis network safehouse").[[21]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_the_Rebellion-21)

At the safehouse, Mothma thanked Andor, before he left to return to Yavin IV with an injured [Wilmon Paak](/wiki/Wilmon_Paak "Wilmon Paak") and [Dreena](/wiki/Dreena "Dreena") of the [Ghorman Front](/wiki/Ghorman_Front "Ghorman Front"). [Kleya Marki](/wiki/Kleya_Marki "Kleya Marki"), Rael's associate, revealed to Mothma that Rael was safe. Marki then handed Mothma, along with Erskin Semaj, over to the [Gold Squadron](/wiki/Gold_Squadron_(Rebel_Alliance) "Gold Squadron (Rebel Alliance)"), a bomber squad associated with Bail Organa that,[[21]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_the_Rebellion-21) for publicity purposes, was encharged with delivering Mothma[[70]](#cite_note-EmmysQA-70) to Dantooine[[69]](#cite_note-Secret_Cargo-69) and then to Yavin as well as rally the current formation of the Rebel Alliance with the message that it was they who had broken Mothma out of the senate.[[21]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_the_Rebellion-21)

Following the escape, ISB agents also visited Cantham House on Coruscant, the meeting place of the [Cantham House meetings](/wiki/Cantham_House_meetings "Cantham House meetings"), based on suspicions they had, and questioned Leia and several others there.[[22]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-22) After being picked up by Gold Squadron, Mothma delivered another speech[[71]](#cite_note-ChangedSpeech-71) in which she denounced the Emperor as a "lying executioner."[[69]](#cite_note-Secret_Cargo-69)

##### Operation Handoff[]

:   "*We're in the process of building an alliance, uniting the various rebel cells across the galaxy. My challenge to the Emperor was a call to stand against the Empire. My hope is, all who answer it will see that they are not alone. I must be there to meet them.*"
:   ―Mothma, to Hera Syndulla[[69]](#cite_note-Secret_Cargo-69)

 [![The Chandrila Mistress docks with the Ghost.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d3/ChandrilaMistress-RebelsS03E18.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170306214523) [![The Chandrila Mistress docks with the Ghost.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d3/ChandrilaMistress-RebelsS03E18.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170306214523)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d3/ChandrilaMistress-RebelsS03E18.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170306214523) 

The *Chandrila Mistress* docks with the *Ghost*.

 

Mothma traveled aboard her [freighter](/wiki/Freighter "Freighter") the *[Chandrila Mistress](/wiki/Chandrila_Mistress "Chandrila Mistress")* with Semaj and her Gold Squadron escort, intending to arrive at Dantooine before a meeting there and broadcast a third speech that would be shown throughout the galaxy, specifically targeting rebel factions that could come together to form the next chapter of the alliance. [Phoenix Leader](/wiki/Phoenix_Leader "Phoenix Leader") [Hera Syndulla](/wiki/Hera_Syndulla "Hera Syndulla")'s crew, who were members of the [Lothal sector](/wiki/Lothal_sector "Lothal sector")-based [Phoenix Cell](/wiki/Phoenix_Cell "Phoenix Cell"), was dispatched by Bail Organa to rendezvous with the *Chandrila Mistress* and provide them with fuel. When Syndulla's crew, known as the [Spectres](/wiki/Spectres "Spectres"), docked their ship, the *Ghost*, with Mothma's ship and started refueling, Semaj kept them in the dark about who the ship was delivering. After the *Chandrila Mistress* was attacked by Imperial forces, she and her crew abandoned their ship and sought refuge aboard the *Ghost*. Mothma helped Syndulla's droid [Chopper](/wiki/C1-10P "C1-10P") to detach the *Ghost* from her stricken freighter.[[69]](#cite_note-Secret_Cargo-69)

After escaping into [hyperspace](/wiki/Hyperspace "Hyperspace"), Hera introduced her crew to Mothma. Mothma praised both [Ezra Bridger](/wiki/Ezra_Bridger "Ezra Bridger"), who was flying [Gold Two's](/wiki/Gold_Two_(rebellion) "Gold Two (rebellion)") Y-wing starfighter, and the [Lasat](/wiki/Lasat "Lasat") Captain [Garazeb Orrelios](/wiki/Garazeb_Orrelios "Garazeb Orrelios") for their services to the rebellion. Ezra thanked Mothma for her speech criticizing the Emperor. When Erskin counseled her to abandon her planned mission to [Dantooine](/wiki/Dantooine "Dantooine"), Mothma refused and argued that she had to be present at the meeting. Mothma then informed the Spectres that she was planning to build an alliance of rebel cells to challenge the Empire and unify the rebellion. After Erskin warned them that the Empire was trying to intercept any ship leaving the system, Hera decided they would travel through the dangerous [Archeon pass](/wiki/Archeon_pass "Archeon pass").[[69]](#cite_note-Secret_Cargo-69)

 [![The Ghost travels through the Archeon Nebula, pursued by Imperials.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5a/Nebula_fight.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170306232014) [![The Ghost travels through the Archeon Nebula, pursued by Imperials.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5a/Nebula_fight.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170306232014)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5a/Nebula_fight.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170306232014) 

The *Ghost* travels through the Archeon Nebula, pursued by Imperials.

 

During the journey, the rebels came under [attack](/wiki/Operation_Handoff "Operation Handoff") from [Grand Admiral](/wiki/Grand_Admiral "Grand Admiral") [Thrawn's](/wiki/Mitth%27raw%27nuruodo "Mitth'raw'nuruodo") prototype [TIE Defender](/wiki/TIE/d_%22Defender%22_Multi-Role_Starfighter "TIE/d \"Defender\" Multi-Role Starfighter") starfighter and two [TIE Interceptors](/wiki/TIE/IN_interceptor "TIE/IN interceptor"). Three Y-wings were lost during the skirmish but the rebels also managed to destroy the two TIE interceptors. While [Gold Leader](/wiki/Gold_Leader "Gold Leader") Captain [Jon Vander](/wiki/Jon_Vander "Jon Vander") and Ezra distracted the TIE Defender, Hera flew the *Ghost* out of the Archeon Nebula only to find their way blocked by two Star Destroyers commanded by Governor [Arihnda Pryce](/wiki/Arihnda_Pryce "Arihnda Pryce") and Admiral [Kassius Konstantine](/wiki/Kassius_Konstantine "Kassius Konstantine").[[69]](#cite_note-Secret_Cargo-69)

While Hera and Chopper readied the *Ghost*'s hyperdrive, Mothma tried to stall Governor Pryce with a list of demands. Pryce however rejected her demands and ordered Konstantine to activate the Star Destroyer's [tractor beam projector](/wiki/Tractor_beam_projector "Tractor beam projector"). Before the *Ghost* could be drawn inside the Star Destroyer, Vander and Ezra emerged from the Archeon Nebula. Under Hera's orders, they fired their [proton torpedoes](/wiki/Proton_torpedo "Proton torpedo") into the nebula. This caused an explosion which badly damaged the two Star Destroyers and allowed the rebels to flee to Dantooine.[[69]](#cite_note-Secret_Cargo-69)

##### Forming the Alliance[]

:   "*This is Senator Mon Mothma, I have been called a traitor for speaking out against a corrupt Galactic Senate. A Senate manipulated by the sinister tactics of the Emperor. For too long I have watched the heavy hand of the Empire strangle our liberties, stifling our freedoms in the name of ensuring our safety. No longer! Despite Imperial threats, despite the Emperor himself, I have no fear as I take new action. For I am not alone. Beginning today we stand together as allies. I hereby resign from the Senate to fight for you, not from the distant hall of politics but from the front lines. We will not rest until we bring an end to the Empire, until we restore our Republic! Are you with me?*"
:   ―Mon Mothma unites the various rebel cells[[69]](#cite_note-Secret_Cargo-69)

 [![Senator Mothma onboard the Ghost.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5e/Secret_Cargo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170302113903) [![Senator Mothma onboard the Ghost.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5e/Secret_Cargo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20170302113903)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/5e/Secret_Cargo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170302113903) 

Senator Mothma onboard the *Ghost*.

 

Above Dantooine, Mon Mothma gave a speech stating that she had resigned from the Imperial Senate since it had been corrupted by the Emperor. With the Senate no longer able to protect the rights and freedom of the galaxy's citizens, she advocated the formation of an Alliance to Restore the Republic. This speech was witnessed by Senator Organa, General [Jan Dodonna](/wiki/Jan_Dodonna "Jan Dodonna"), and members of [Ryder Azadi](/wiki/Ryder_Azadi "Ryder Azadi")'s [Lothal resistance group](/wiki/Lothal_resistance_group "Lothal resistance group") and Phoenix Squadron. Shortly later, the [rebel fleet](/wiki/Rebel_Alliance_Navy "Rebel Alliance Navy") emerged from hyperspace above Dantooine and the Alliance was formed,[[69]](#cite_note-Secret_Cargo-69) officially beginning the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War").[[72]](#cite_note-Insider_203-72) Members of the [Alliance Military](/wiki/Alliance_Military "Alliance Military") would nickname Mothma "Double-M."[[73]](#cite_note-Rendezvous_Point-73) Mothma was then eventually delivered to Yavin, as Gold Squadron had originally intended.[[21]](#cite_note-Welcome_to_the_Rebellion-21)

#### Pragmatism[]

:   "*Senator, there must be someone you can send or something you can do."*  
    "*I wish I could help you, Commander Bridger, but I can't. Doing so would play into Thrawn's hands, and he would wipe out all we've worked to build."*  
    "*I know. He planned this."*  
    "*Senator Organa was right. It was too soon for open warfare against the Empire. I promise you, we will do our best to negotiate fair treatment for the prisoners."*  
    "*What if there are no prisoners? I'm not ready to give up yet."*  
    "*You have courage, Ezra. May the Force be with you.*"
:   ―Ezra Bridger and Senator Mon Mothma discussing the Battle of Atollon[[74]](#cite_note-Zero_Hour-74)

After escaping Grand Admiral Thrawn's [siege](/wiki/Battle_of_Atollon "Battle of Atollon") of [Atollon](/wiki/Atollon "Atollon"), Ezra contacted Mon Mothma via hologram and tried to solicit her help in sending reinforcements to aid the besieged Phoenix Squadron and General Dodonna's [Massassi Group](/wiki/Massassi_Group "Massassi Group"). However, the rebel leader was unwilling to expose the true strength of the Rebel Alliance to Thrawn and admitted that the Alliance was not yet ready for open warfare against the Empire. When Mothma promised to negotiate fair treatment for the prisoners, Ezra warned that Thrawn might not take prisoners. Before exiting the conversation, Mothma complimented Ezra for his courage and wished that [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force") would be with him. Ultimately, the rebels managed to escape Atollon with the help of [Mandalorians](/wiki/Mandalorian "Mandalorian") from [Clan Wren](/wiki/Clan_Wren "Clan Wren").[[74]](#cite_note-Zero_Hour-74)

#### Mission to Jalindi[]

:   "*You target civilians, kill those who surrender, break every rule of engagement! If we degrade ourselves to the Empire's level, what will we become?*"  
    "*There she is! That's the leader the Rebellion needs! Where is that fire, that passion, when your people need it most? I hope, Senator, after you've lost, and the Empire reigns over the galaxy unopposed, you will find some comfort in the knowledge that you fought according to the rules.*"
:   ―Mon Mothma and Saw Gerrera[[75]](#cite_note-In_the_Name_of_Rebellion-75)

In the aftermath of Atollon, the full Rebel Alliance relocated to the [Yavin rebel base](/wiki/Great_Temple "Great Temple") on [Yavin 4](/wiki/Yavin_4 "Yavin 4").[[75]](#cite_note-In_the_Name_of_Rebellion-75) Around [1 BBY](/wiki/1_BBY "1 BBY"),[[76]](#cite_note-Jalindi_Date-76) following Phoenix squadron's return from a failed supply mission, Mothma welcomed Hera Syndulla at the subsequent meeting, commending her bravery. After Bail Organa attributed their faulty intelligence to a new Imperial satellite [relay](/wiki/Jalindi_Station "Jalindi Station") on [Jalindi](/wiki/Jalindi "Jalindi"), Ezra remarked on [Saw Gerrera](/wiki/Saw_Gerrera "Saw Gerrera")'s more extreme methods of acquiring the information, to which Mothma was quick to remind him the rest of the Rebellion does not torture prisoners. When [Alexsandr Kallus](/wiki/Alexsandr_Kallus "Alexsandr Kallus") suggested intercepting the satellite relay, Mothma agreed to the plan and placed Hera in charge of the [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Jalindi "Mission to Jalindi"). At the meeting's conclusion, Ezra once again pleaded for Mothma's help in liberating Lothal. Though sympathetic to the planet's plight as much as other worlds under Imperial control, Mothma reminded Ezra the Rebellion was not yet strong enough to do so.[[75]](#cite_note-In_the_Name_of_Rebellion-75)

 [![Mothma speaks to Saw Gerrera via hologram regarding the Alliance's tactics.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4b/In_the_Name_-_Saw_Speaks.png/revision/latest?cb=20180121041103) [![Mothma speaks to Saw Gerrera via hologram regarding the Alliance's tactics.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4b/In_the_Name_-_Saw_Speaks.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20180121041103)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4b/In_the_Name_-_Saw_Speaks.png/revision/latest?cb=20180121041103) 

Mothma speaks to Saw Gerrera via hologram regarding the Alliance's tactics.

 

That night, Saw appeared via hologram from an astromech droid, denouncing the leaders of the Alliance. Mothma was quick to respond, demanding to know his reasons for contacting them. When Gerrera reminded her of her refusal to destroy the Jalindi relay, Mothma in turn refused to fall to his level, reminding Saw of his numerous war crimes. Reminding her that the Empire viewed them both as criminals, Gerrera warned that playing by the rules would be the death of the Rebellion. Despite their conversation, the relay was inevitably destroyed by Gerrera and the *Ghost* crew following the unexpected arrival of [Brom Titus](/wiki/Brom_Titus "Brom Titus").[[75]](#cite_note-In_the_Name_of_Rebellion-75)

#### Raid on Lothal[]

Weeks later, Mothma informed Ezra of a message from Azadi concerning a new development of the TIE Defender. Having witnessed the ships in action firsthand, Mothma asked for Ezra's [help in](/wiki/Theft_of_the_TIE_Defender_Elite "Theft of the TIE Defender Elite") gathering intelligence on Lothal. Bridger and the rest of the *Ghost* crew readily agreed, though Mothma could not guarantee their extraction due to the Empire's massive blockade.[[77]](#cite_note-Occupation-77) After Hera and Chopper acquired the [TIE/D Defender Elite](/wiki/TIE/D_Defender_Elite "TIE/D Defender Elite")'s [flight data recorder](/wiki/Flight_data_recorder "Flight data recorder") and returned to Yavin 4, Mothma and Erskin Semaj greeted the two rebels.[[78]](#cite_note-Kindred-78)

Mon Mothma later attended a briefing with General Dodonna, Senator Organa, Semaj, and Syndulla to discuss the flight data recorder. During the meeting, Hera urged Mothma to launch a [strike](/wiki/Attack_on_Lothal "Attack on Lothal") on the Imperial TIE Defender factories on Lothal and added that she had a ground strike team. Mothma responded by asking her and Chopper to wait outside while she discussed the matter. In private, Mothma and the others discussed [Protocol 13](/wiki/Protocol_13 "Protocol 13"). Hera re-entered the meeting and urged the rebel leadership to launch the strike. Mothma was swayed and authorized Syndulla's strike.[[79]](#cite_note-Crawler_Commandeers-79) However, Syndulla's squadron of [X-wing starfighters](/wiki/X-wing_starfighter "X-wing starfighter") was intercepted and largely wiped out by Thrawn's Seventh Fleet.[[80]](#cite_note-Rebel_Assault-80)

#### The Mustafar operation[]

:   "*This is Mon Mothma. I have an assignment for you. The Rebellion needs you and we don't have much time. You must work together. You must not fail. In disguise, your team's mission is to recover Imperial intelligence critical to our survival.*"
:   ―Mon Mothma[[81]](#cite_note-Trailer-81)

Before or during 1 BBY,[[82]](#cite_note-SotE_Date-82) Mon Mothma assigned a group of operatives to an intelligence [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar_(Rebel_Alliance) "Mission to Mustafar (Rebel Alliance)") to [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar"), which she deemed critical to the Rebellion's survival.[[81]](#cite_note-Trailer-81)

#### Death Star plans[]

:   "*We need to stop this weapon before it's finished.*"
:   ―Mon Mothma, to Jyn Erso[[17]](#cite_note-Rogue_One-17)

 [![Mon Mothma on Yavin 4, shortly before the outbreak of the Galactic Civil War.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c5/Mon_Mothma_on_Yavin_4.png/revision/latest?cb=20160407140434) [![Mon Mothma on Yavin 4, shortly before the outbreak of the Galactic Civil War.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c5/Mon_Mothma_on_Yavin_4.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20160407140434)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c5/Mon_Mothma_on_Yavin_4.png/revision/latest?cb=20160407140434) 

Mon Mothma on Yavin 4, shortly before the outbreak of the Galactic Civil War.

 

By [1 BBY](/wiki/1_BBY "1 BBY"),[[83]](#cite_note-Timelines-83) Mon Mothma had become [Chancellor](/wiki/Chancellor_(Rebel_Alliance) "Chancellor (Rebel Alliance)")[[84]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_4-84) and [Commander-in-Chief](/wiki/Commander-in-Chief "Commander-in-Chief") of the Rebel Alliance. As leader of the Alliance, Mothma was privy to [Operation Fracture](/wiki/Operation_Fracture "Operation Fracture"),[[85]](#cite_note-Rogue_One_Rebel_Dossier-85) a secret operation to extract the [scientist](/wiki/Scientist "Scientist") [Galen Erso](/wiki/Galen_Walton_Erso "Galen Walton Erso") so that he could testify to the Imperial Senate regarding the existence of a planet-destroying [superweapon](/wiki/Superweapon "Superweapon") called the [Death Star](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station"). The Alliance had learned about the existence of the Death Star from the defecting Imperial pilot [Bodhi Rook](/wiki/Bodhi_Rook "Bodhi Rook"), who had been captured by Gerrera's [Partisans](/wiki/Partisans "Partisans").[[17]](#cite_note-Rogue_One-17)

Operation Fracture involved the Alliance rescuing Galen's daughter [Jyn Erso](/wiki/Jyn_Erso "Jyn Erso") so that the Alliance could make contact with Gerrera and question Rook about the Death Star and Galen's location. The Alliance also needed Jyn to verify Galen's identity. When General [Davits Draven](/wiki/Davits_Draven "Davits Draven") objected to Jyn's presence on the Operation Fraction team due to her criminal and violent tendencies, Mothma countered that Jyn was essential to identifying Galen and persuading him to testify in the Senate about the Death Star. While recognizing Jyn's criminal tendencies, Mothma argued that everybody including criminals and outcasts deserved a second chance.[[85]](#cite_note-Rogue_One_Rebel_Dossier-85)

Mothma also supported General Draven's recommendation that Captain [Cassian Andor](/wiki/Cassian_Jeron_Andor "Cassian Jeron Andor") be assigned to Operation Fracture. While describing him as one of the best and brightest rebel operatives, Mothma expressed concerns that rebel fighters like Andor had to grapple with doing terrible things in the course of their services to the Rebellion. In addition, Mon Mothma was also briefed about several topics including Galen Erso's expertise on crystal science and energy generation, suspected Imperial disinformation, speculation about the Empire's planned weapons test, Grand Moff Tarkin, and Alliance military assets by various colleagues including General Draven, Senator [Nower Jebel](/wiki/Nower_Jebel "Nower Jebel"), [Advisor](/wiki/Advisor "Advisor") [Hostis Ij](/wiki/Hostis_Ij "Hostis Ij"), General Jan Dodonna, and Admiral [Raddus](/wiki/Raddus "Raddus").[[85]](#cite_note-Rogue_One_Rebel_Dossier-85)

Jyn convinced Saw to show her the message, which detailed the superweapon's destructive power and a weakness that Galen had deliberately set in the station. He also explained that a copy of the weapon's technical readouts were kept in the [Citadel Tower](/wiki/Citadel_Tower "Citadel Tower") on [Scarif](/wiki/Scarif "Scarif"). Jyn was unable to deliver the holographic recording to the Alliance due the [Destruction of Jedha City](/wiki/Destruction_of_Jedha_City "Destruction of Jedha City"). Erso and Andor were able to escape [Jedha](/wiki/Jedha "Jedha"), and set course for [Eadu](/wiki/Eadu "Eadu"). En route, Andor relayed news of Jedha's destruction, while General Draven confirmed his orders to kill Galen Erso.[[17]](#cite_note-Rogue_One-17)

Andor's U-wing crashed on Eadu because of the planet's foul weather. The loss of contact with Andor and his team forced Draven to launch a [mission to Eadu](/wiki/Mission_to_Eadu "Mission to Eadu"), which succeeded at killing Galen Erso. Following the return of Andor's team to the Massassi base, Mothma led a discussion among the Alliance's leaders regarding the future of the rebellion. Despite knowing that full-scale war against the Empire was inevitable and wanting to escalate the fight, Mothma followed the recommendations of the council and denied Jyn Erso permission to launch a mission to retrieve the [Death Star plans](/wiki/Death_Star_plans "Death Star plans"). Mothma and Organa knew that war was unavoidable, and sought to bring as many allies to their cause as they could. While Mothma remained on Base One, Organa tasked his subordinates and Leia to prepare to go to Tatooine. Erso, Andor, and their crew disobeyed her orders and formed the [Rogue One](/wiki/Rogue_One "Rogue One") [squad](/wiki/Squad "Squad"), which fired the opening shots of the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War") at the [Battle of Scarif](/wiki/Battle_of_Scarif "Battle of Scarif"). When Base One intercepted communications that there were rebel actions on Scarif, Mothma was walking with Generals Dravin and [Antoc Merrick](/wiki/Antoc_Merrick "Antoc Merrick") when informed. Mothma requested to speak with Admiral Raddus, but was told that he's gone to his vessel, the *[Profundity](/wiki/Profundity "Profundity")* and that they were going to fight. Rogue One's actions led to the intervention of the Alliance Fleet, which allowed the successful theft and transmissions of the plans to the *Profundity* and Leia's ship, the *[Tantive IV](/wiki/Tantive_IV "Tantive IV")*.[[17]](#cite_note-Rogue_One-17)

Shortly thereafter, the Empire used the Death Star to [destroy](/wiki/Destruction_of_Alderaan "Destruction of Alderaan") Alderaan,[[86]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-86) killing Bail and Breha Organa with it.[[1]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-1) Mothma became the sole political leader of the Rebel Alliance,[[4]](#cite_note-Databank-4) serving as its own chancellor throughout the Galactic Civil War.[[84]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_4-84) As the Rebel Alliance awaited Leia Organa's success or failure in delivering the Death Star plans, Mothma prepared multiple contingency plans and gathered intelligence resources. Due to the possibility that a rebel assault on the Death Star would end in defeat, Mothma's survival would ensure the rebellion lived on. Her aide [Cianne](/wiki/Cianne "Cianne") accompanied her as she departed in a shuttle. Mothma was in the process of writing a surrender speech she may have to deliver to Emperor Palpatine and his Empire when she received the news that the rebels had won.[[87]](#cite_note-Contingency_Plan-87)

#### After Yavin[]

After the Battle of Yavin, in which Luke Skywalker, who had become a Rebel pilot, destroyed the Death Star and prevented the annihilation of the Rebel Alliance,[[86]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-86) the Alliance debated trying to convince the [Chekkoo clan](/wiki/Chekkoo_clan "Chekkoo clan") of Rodia to join the Rebellion. Mothma was unsure of the idea, but Ackbar and Leia Organa agreed with it, and it was eventually decided they would send Skywalker on the [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Rodia_(Luke_Skywalker) "Mission to Rodia (Luke Skywalker)").[[88]](#cite_note-Heir_to_the_Jedi-88) Mothma later sent Skywalker on a [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_recover_Imperial_communication_logs "Mission to recover Imperial communication logs") to retrieve logs of Imperial communications that were intercepted by several rebel cells along the [Shipwrights' Trace](/wiki/Shipwrights%27_Trace "Shipwrights' Trace").[[89]](#cite_note-weapon-jedi-89)

At some point later, the [Alliance High Command](/wiki/Alliance_High_Command "Alliance High Command") met in the Alliance Fleet to discuss what actions to take next. Organa, who had just completed a successful [assault](/wiki/Assault_on_Cymoon "Assault on Cymoon") on [Weapons Factory Alpha](/wiki/Weapons_Factory_Alpha "Weapons Factory Alpha") on [Cymoon 1](/wiki/Cymoon_1 "Cymoon 1"), urged the leadership to allow her team to continue pressing the Alliance's advantage against the Empire. Admiral [Gial Ackbar](/wiki/Gial_Ackbar "Gial Ackbar") told the princess that they could not maintain such an offensive due to still being on the run, a stance that Mothma agreed with. The chancellor said that the few resources that they had must be put towards keeping the fleet moving so the Empire could not find them. Only by establishing a new base, Mothma said, would they be able to change that stance. Concerned for the well-being of her old friend, Mothma also reminded the princess that she could not afford to continue pushing herself or her team so hard in the fight against the Empire.[[84]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_4-84)

 [![Mothma served as chancellor of the Rebel Alliance and a member of the Alliance High Command.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f0/AllianceHighCommand-2015StarWars9.png/revision/latest?cb=20151004015825) [![Mothma served as chancellor of the Rebel Alliance and a member of the Alliance High Command.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f0/AllianceHighCommand-2015StarWars9.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20151004015825)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f0/AllianceHighCommand-2015StarWars9.png/revision/latest?cb=20151004015825) 

Mothma served as chancellor of the Rebel Alliance and a member of the Alliance High Command.

 

High Command later received word that Skywalker had been captured by [Grakkus](/wiki/Grakkus_Jahibakti_Tingi "Grakkus Jahibakti Tingi"), a Hutt crime lord, on the [moon](/wiki/Moon "Moon") of [Nar Shaddaa](/wiki/Nar_Shaddaa "Nar Shaddaa"). Despite Skywalker's value to the Alliance and his status as the hero of the Battle of Yavin, Mothma made the difficult choice to decide against using any large amount of Alliance resources to rescue him, knowing that the Rebellion could not move against a Hutt stronghold. She also believed that sending a covert team would be a suicide mission. Nonetheless, Skywalker's [Wookiee](/wiki/Wookiee "Wookiee") friend [Chewbacca](/wiki/Chewbacca "Chewbacca") and [protocol droid](/wiki/Protocol_droid "Protocol droid") [C-3PO](/wiki/C-3PO "C-3PO") agreed to travel to Nar Shaddaa to help the captive Rebel.[[90]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_9-90) With help from Organa, the [smuggler](/wiki/Smuggler "Smuggler")-turned-Rebel [Han Solo](/wiki/Han_Solo "Han Solo"), and [astromech droid](/wiki/Astromech_droid "Astromech droid") [R2-D2](/wiki/R2-D2 "R2-D2"), who rendezvoused with them on Nar Shaddaa, Chewbacca and Threepio successfully rescued Skywalker.[[91]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_12-91) Despite the valuable victory at Yavin, the Alliance remained on the back foot as the Empire's full fury was brought down on the rebels. Offensives in the [Mid Rim](/wiki/Mid_Rim_Territories "Mid Rim Territories") turned into [retreat](/wiki/Mid_Rim_Retreat "Mid Rim Retreat"), and the personal toll on Mothma throughout the war was heavy, but she remained steadfast.[[28]](#cite_note-HC_40-28)

After Alliance forces managed to shoot down [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Vader onto the planet [Vrogas Vas](/wiki/Vrogas_Vas "Vrogas Vas") during the [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Vrogas_Vas "Battle of Vrogas Vas"), Mothma approved of Leia's request for a coordinated Alliance strike on the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") [Lord](/wiki/Lord "Lord"), stating that his capture was preferable but eliminating him was acceptable.[[22]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-22) Later, Mothma attended an Alliance High Command meeting in which Skywalker and Organa suggested that the Alliance attempt to [hijack](/wiki/Hijacking_of_the_Harbinger "Hijacking of the Harbinger") an [*Imperial*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Harbinger_(Imperial_I-class) "Harbinger (Imperial I-class)") in order to break the [Siege on Tureen VII](/wiki/Siege_on_Tureen_VII "Siege on Tureen VII"). Mothma was skeptical of the plan, but ultimately approved it due to Skywalker and Organa's reputation.[[92]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_23-92)

#### Battle of Hoth and aftermath[]

As the Alliance focused on building their new Alliance High Command headquarters in [Echo Base](/wiki/Echo_Base "Echo Base") on [Hoth](/wiki/Hoth "Hoth"), Chancellor Mon Mothma was present on the *[Home One](/wiki/Home_One "Home One")* alongside [Admiral](/wiki/Admiral "Admiral") [Gial Ackbar](/wiki/Gial_Ackbar "Gial Ackbar"), [General](/wiki/General "General") [Crix Madine](/wiki/Crix_Madine "Crix Madine"), and others when [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") [Beilert Valance](/wiki/Beilert_Valance "Beilert Valance") provided the Rebellion with the plans for a [shield generator](/wiki/Deflector_shield_generator "Deflector shield generator") that could withstand [orbital bombardment](/wiki/Orbital_bombardment "Orbital bombardment"). When questioned about the [engineer](/wiki/Engineer "Engineer") who was supposed to bring them the plans, Valance informed them that he didn't make it, and expected to be paid half of the credits he was owed. Mothma asked about him being paid half, to which Valance said that the other half would be for the ransom for the engineer's family that was held by the Empire.[[93]](#cite_note-Empire_Ascendant_1-93) By this time, General Madine had quickly become a valued advisor to Mothma.[[94]](#cite_note-HC_23-94)

One night at Echo Base, General [Carlist Rieekan](/wiki/Carlist_Rieekan "Carlist Rieekan") was off-world with Mothma, leaving General Leia Organa in command of the base. At that time, the heaters failed and Leia had to place everyone in starships as a temporary measure and evacuate the base when the [reactor](/wiki/Reactor "Reactor") was briefly compromised.[[95]](#cite_note-SW_2020_12-95) Echo Base was eventually discovered by the Galactic Empire, commencing the [Battle of Hoth](/wiki/Battle_of_Hoth "Battle of Hoth") when the Imperial [Death Squadron](/wiki/Death_Squadron "Death Squadron") arrived and landed [Blizzard Force](/wiki/Blizzard_Force "Blizzard Force"). Generals Rieekan and Leia Organa commanded the Alliance forces, which[[96]](#cite_note-Episode_V-96) at the time of the battle, had more than 7,500 personnel at the base. The Alliance command staff, including Chancellor Mothma, had not yet arrived when the battle began.[[97]](#cite_note-HC_32-97)

Following the battle, Mothma met Lieutenant [Thane Kyrell](/wiki/Thane_Kyrell "Thane Kyrell"), an Imperial-turned-Rebel, after he had become intoxicated following a night of drinking. Though he did not know who she was, Mothma helped find a chair so he could sit down, and he told her all about how he had defected from the Empire but still loved [Ciena Ree](/wiki/Ciena_Ree "Ciena Ree"), a childhood friend turned lover who served in the [Imperial Navy](/wiki/Imperial_Navy "Imperial Navy"). Mothma listened to his story, including how he was afraid that he might shoot Ree down in battle someday and that he did not want to let his fellow Rebels down for fear of killing the woman he loved. The next morning, Mothma briefed Kyrell and other pilots on a mission they were to carry out for the Alliance. At the end of the briefing, Mothma spoke to Kyrell, who apologized for his actions the previous night. Mothma told him that she did not drum anyone out of the Alliance for getting intoxicated once in a while, lest there be no Rebellion left to fight the Empire, but she did want to know he was capable of doing his duty. He assured her that he was, and he took heed of her words that it was acceptable to love someone on the other side of the war so long as he loved the cause of the Rebel Alliance more.[[98]](#cite_note-Lost_Stars-98)

In the aftermath of their defeat at Hoth, the Alliance Navy split into naval [divisions](/wiki/Division "Division").[[99]](#cite_note-SW_2020_15-99) After she spent a time with[[73]](#cite_note-Rendezvous_Point-73) the [Seventh Division](/wiki/Seventh_Division "Seventh Division")[[100]](#cite_note-SW_2020_8-100) aboard the rebel flagship *Home One*,[[73]](#cite_note-Rendezvous_Point-73) Mon Mothma, along with Admiral Ackbar and the [Eleventh Division](/wiki/Eleventh_Division "Eleventh Division"), found herself blockaded by the Galactic Empire on [Ab Dalis](/wiki/Ab_Dalis "Ab Dalis") when they were discovered. During the [Battle of Ab Dalis](/wiki/Battle_of_Ab_Dalis "Battle of Ab Dalis"), [Colonel](/wiki/Colonel "Colonel") [Chouch](/wiki/Chouch "Chouch") and the [Ground Defense Command](/wiki/Ground_Defense_Command "Ground Defense Command") protected Mothma and the Eleventh Division's ships until [Starlight Squadron](/wiki/Starlight_Squadron "Starlight Squadron") from the [Fourth Division](/wiki/Fourth_Division "Fourth Division") arrived to reinforce them. After destroying the *[Ultima II](/wiki/Ultima_II "Ultima II")*, Mothma thanked the pilots of Starlight Squadron, and that now they would be able to join the fight.[[99]](#cite_note-SW_2020_15-99)

#### The Death Star II[]

:   "*Luke…what is it? What do you need to tell us?*"  
    "*The Empire's building another Death Star.*"  
    "*If we could do it once…we can do it again. Let's get to work.*"
:   ―Mon Mothma and Luke Skywalker[[101]](#cite_note-SW_2020_28-101)

 [![Luke Skywalker reveals the existence of the Death Star II to Mothma, Syndulla, and Ackbar.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/LukeRevealsDeathStarII-2020StarWars28.png/revision/latest?cb=20231105153423) [![Luke Skywalker reveals the existence of the Death Star II to Mothma, Syndulla, and Ackbar.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/LukeRevealsDeathStarII-2020StarWars28.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20231105153423)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/LukeRevealsDeathStarII-2020StarWars28.png/revision/latest?cb=20231105153423) 

Luke Skywalker reveals the existence of the Death Star II to Mothma, Syndulla, and Ackbar.

 

Eventually, Luke Skywalker decided to pursue a distress call from two individuals, [Bevelyn](/wiki/Bevelyn "Bevelyn") and [Jon Melton](/wiki/Jon_Melton "Jon Melton") who claimed to be former Imperials. After rescuing them and their children, Skywalker learned that they had worked as double agents for the Empire-antagonistic [Crimson Dawn](/wiki/Crimson_Dawn "Crimson Dawn") criminal syndicate, and revealed that they had been stationed on a [second Death Star](/wiki/DS-2_Death_Star_II_Mobile_Battle_Station "DS-2 Death Star II Mobile Battle Station") that the Empire was building. Skywalker then met with Mothma, General Syndulla, and Admiral Ackbar and told them who the Meltons were. Ackbar was concerned about Crimson Dawn having spies within the Alliance, but Mothma was more interested in the news Skywalker had brought. When the Jedi-in-training revealed that the Empire was building another Death Star, a shocked Mothma declared that they had defeated the first Death Star, and would defeat the new one as well.[[101]](#cite_note-SW_2020_28-101)

[Three years](/wiki/3_ABY "3 ABY") after the Battle of Yavin,[[20]](#cite_note-Moving_Target-20) Mothma depressingly passed on the information provided to her from the [Bothan Spynet](/wiki/Bothan_Spynet "Bothan Spynet") to her senior commanders and advisors, and that what she told them had to remain secret as she knew that after the defeat at Hoth, news of the [DS-2 Death Star II Mobile Battle Station](/wiki/DS-2_Death_Star_II_Mobile_Battle_Station "DS-2 Death Star II Mobile Battle Station") could shatter the Alliance.[[94]](#cite_note-HC_23-94) Knowing that the information leak was likely a trap, Mothma and her military advisors had no choice but to fully commit the Alliance in destroying the station and the Emperor.[[28]](#cite_note-HC_40-28) The Alliance learned that the [battle station](/wiki/Battle_station "Battle station") was in the [orbit](/wiki/Orbit "Orbit") of the [Forest](/wiki/Tree "Tree") Moon of [Endor](/wiki/Endor "Endor") and under construction. Mothma met with the Alliance High Command to discuss strategy for how to deal with the threat of a new Death Star, and it was agreed that the [battle station](/wiki/Battle_station "Battle station") had to be destroyed before it was fully operational. The leadership began planning for an assault on the Death Star II over Endor, but first the Alliance Fleet, which had broken up following the Rebellion's defeat during the Battle of [Hoth](/wiki/Hoth "Hoth")—Mothma insisted that it break into smaller groups to avoid another disaster that the Empire could celebrate—would have to regroup near [Sullust](/wiki/Sullust "Sullust"). Organa volunteered to lead an operation, codenamed [Operation Yellow Moon](/wiki/Operation_Yellow_Moon "Operation Yellow Moon"), to distract Imperial forces while the Alliance Fleet gathered together. Mothma was opposed to the idea at first, and she spoke with the princess about her concerns—concerns stemming from Organa's willingness to sacrifice herself for the Alliance.[[20]](#cite_note-Moving_Target-20) Although Madine provided the idea of training commando infiltration teams to sabotage the station from within, Mothma did not want to delay as she feared that entire worlds would be destroyed before they were ready.[[94]](#cite_note-HC_23-94)

The chancellor knew that Organa was in love with Captain Solo, who had been taken captive by [Jabba](/wiki/Jabba_Desilijic_Tiure "Jabba Desilijic Tiure") the Hutt months earlier, and worried that Organa was willing to sacrifice happiness to die for the Rebel cause. Mothma also knew that Organa blamed herself for the destruction of Alderaan, so she told the princess a piece of intelligence: the Emperor intended to use the new Death Star to destroy worlds such as [Mon Cala](/wiki/Mon_Cala "Mon Cala") and even Chandrila, all to eliminate opposition to his rule. Mothma knew that if she allowed herself to be ruled by such fears, she would not be able to serve the Alliance. The chancellor approved Operation Yellow Moon, and urged her young friend not to deny herself an opportunity for love—a love denied because of total devotion to the Alliance—because of what happened to her parents and to Alderaan. Operation Yellow Moon was successful and the Alliance Fleet gathered near Sullust.[[20]](#cite_note-Moving_Target-20)

#### The Battle of Endor[]

:   "*The Emperor has made a critical error and the time for our attack has come.*"
:   ―Mon Mothma, just before the Battle of Endor[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-6)

 [![Mothma briefs the Rebel Alliance on the plan for the Battle of Endor.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b3/Mothmaleadingbriefing.png/revision/latest?cb=20130404024511) [![Mothma briefs the Rebel Alliance on the plan for the Battle of Endor.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b3/Mothmaleadingbriefing.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20130404024511)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b3/Mothmaleadingbriefing.png/revision/latest?cb=20130404024511) 

Mothma briefs the Rebel Alliance on the plan for the Battle of Endor.

 

When it was assembled, the High Command addressed Rebel forces aboard *[Home One](/wiki/Home_One "Home One")*, the Rebel command ship, and shared the existence of the second Death Star. Mothma also revealed that the Emperor himself was personally overseeing the completion of the station's construction. During the briefing, Admiral Ackbar and General Crix Madine outlined the plan of attack. General Solo was picked to lead a ground assault to destroy the [shield generator](/wiki/Death_Star%27s_shield_generator "Death Star's shield generator") protecting the Death Star, while Organa, Chewbacca, and Skywalker volunteered to accompany him.[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-6) After the briefing, Mothma spoke to Organa and expressed concern that the princess had volunteered for the mission.[[102]](#cite_note-Beware_the_Power-102) As with Operation Yellow Moon[[20]](#cite_note-Moving_Target-20) and the [rescue](/wiki/Rescue_of_Han_Solo "Rescue of Han Solo") of General Solo from Jabba the Hutt, Mothma feared that Organa was putting herself, a valuable member of the Alliance and the future republic that they hoped to build, at too great a risk. Mothma shared a story of how, after the Empire's [massacre](/wiki/Massacre_on_Kashyyyk "Massacre on Kashyyyk") on the Wookiee homeworld of [Kashyyyk](/wiki/Kashyyyk "Kashyyyk"), she thought that diplomacy was dead and she trained as a [starfighter](/wiki/Starfighter "Starfighter") [pilot](/wiki/Pilot "Pilot") in order to fight against the Empire. She realized, however, that while she could have helped win a battle, she could contribute more as the leader of the Alliance. Despite Mothma's concerns, which the princess understood, Organa felt it was her destiny to be part of the Battle of Endor and chose to accompany the Rebel forces to the Forest Moon.[[102]](#cite_note-Beware_the_Power-102)

Before the Alliance Fleet left for Endor, Mothma's ship departed so she could be taken to a safe location.[[102]](#cite_note-Beware_the_Power-102) Mothma considered traveling to the rebel-friendly planet [Durkteel](/wiki/Durkteel "Durkteel") to help distract from the attack on the Death Star, but her closest aide, [Hendri Underholt](/wiki/Hendri_Underholt "Hendri Underholt"), convinced her not to take the risk: as Underholt reasoned, she could go with a detachment and, being Mothma's closest aide, it would look like the rebel leader was present without needing to personally arrive. In what would end up being Mothma's final message to Underholt, she thanked her aide for her friendship and the leadership she displayed. Underholt's proposal to Mothma ultimately saved the rebel leader's life: the Empire dispatched three [Star Destroyers](/wiki/Star_Destroyer "Star Destroyer") to Durkteel and [bombarded the planet](/wiki/Bombardment_of_Durkteel "Bombardment of Durkteel"), with Underholt dying in the attack.[[22]](#cite_note-Rebel_Files-22) Meanwhile, the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor") commenced once the Rebel forces arrived over the Forest Moon. Unknown to the Rebellion was that the Emperor had allowed them to learn of the station's existence to lure the Rebels into a trap meant to destroy them once and for all. However, the Alliance emerged victorious: the second Death Star was destroyed, the Emperor was killed,[[6]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-6) and the Empire was left leaderless and in chaos. The tide had turned in the war against the Empire.[[103]](#cite_note-Shattered_Empire_1-103)

### New Republic[]

#### Creating a new order[]

:   "*I've seen war. I know its shape. I know its margins. But I'll never be comfortable with it. It is our fault and we must act that way to uphold our responsibilities. And it's why the war must stop soon. We cannot keep fighting it.*"
:   ―Mon Mothma, shortly after the death of Emperor Palpatine[[18]](#cite_note-Aftermath-18)

Twenty [days](/wiki/Standard_day "Standard day") after the Battle of Endor, Mothma tasked Organa with traveling to Naboo in order to gather support for the formation of a [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic"). Organa was reluctant to leave her other duties and recommended that Mothma send diplomats in her place, but the chancellor believed that Organa's skill and reputation were essential for the mission as the princess represented the best that the Rebel Alliance had to offer. Organa, along with her assigned pilot, Lieutenant [Shara Bey](/wiki/Shara_Bey "Shara Bey"), departed for the mission. Their time there coincided with the Empire launching an attack against the planet, as part of [Operation: Cinder](/wiki/Operation:_Cinder "Operation: Cinder"),[[104]](#cite_note-Shattered_Empire_2-104) but Organa and Bey fought alongside [Queen](/wiki/Monarch_of_Naboo "Monarch of Naboo") [Sosha Soruna](/wiki/Sosha_Soruna "Sosha Soruna") to repel the Imperial attack.[[105]](#cite_note-Shattered_Empire_3-105) The Alliance continued fighting back against other strikes in Operation: Cinder for months.[[106]](#cite_note-Shattered_Empire_4-106)

 [![The formation of the New Republic achieved the goal of the Rebel Alliance.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/New_Republic_canon.svg/revision/latest?cb=20160126010008) [![The formation of the New Republic achieved the goal of the Rebel Alliance.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/New_Republic_canon.svg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160126010008)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0f/New_Republic_canon.svg/revision/latest?cb=20160126010008) 

The formation of the New Republic achieved the goal of the Rebel Alliance.

 

The Alliance formed the New Republic in the months following the Battle of Endor. The [Galactic Senate](/wiki/New_Republic_Senate "New Republic Senate") was reestablished and headquartered on Chandrila, as the New Republic felt that Chandrila represented a planet with big ideas that the Republic would need in order to be successful. Mothma was elected as the first [chancellor](/wiki/Chancellor_(New_Republic) "Chancellor (New Republic)") of the New Republic Senate, and, to her great reluctance, the charter of the chancellor included the emergency powers that had once been given to Palpatine during the Clone Wars. It was Mothma's intention to do away with those powers, believing them to be a poison to democracy. Mothma also planned to propose a massive military disarmament once the Galactic Civil War came to end, hoping to cut the size of the [New Republic Defense Fleet](/wiki/New_Republic_Defense_Fleet "New Republic Defense Fleet") by ninety percent. The other ten percent would go towards training and supporting local militias, which would be responsible for the defense of their worlds. She proposed to put these ideas on the agenda of the first meeting of the reconstituted Senate.[[18]](#cite_note-Aftermath-18)

Later, Chancellor Mothma corresponded via hologram with Admiral Ackbar, General Crix Madine, [Commander](/wiki/Commander "Commander") [Kyrsta Agate](/wiki/Kyrsta_Agate "Kyrsta Agate"), and Captain [Saff Melor](/wiki/Saff_Melor "Saff Melor"). The New Republic officers discussed the disappearance of Captain [Wedge Antilles](/wiki/Wedge_Antilles "Wedge Antilles") during a [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Akiva "Mission to Akiva") to [Akiva](/wiki/Akiva "Akiva") and the reliability of an Imperial informant known as [the Operator](/wiki/Gallius_Rax "Gallius Rax"). When Melor advocated sending military ships to Akiva as a show of force, Mothma cautioned against it because she did not want to promote an aggressive image of the New Republic in the Outer Rim Territories.[[18]](#cite_note-Aftermath-18)

Captain Melor disagreed with the Chancellor and argued that Akiva was a marginal world whose [government](/wiki/Satrapy_of_Myrra "Satrapy of Myrra") were allies of the Empire. In response, Mothma countered that the people outweighed strategic and political considerations. Mothma revealed she had intelligence of a [rebellion](/wiki/Rebellion_on_Akiva "Rebellion on Akiva") on Akiva; which she attributed to the success of the New Republic's messaging campaign. Admiral Ackbar agreed with the Chancellor's assessment. As a compromise, he proposed sending a small strike team of [New Republic Special Forces](/wiki/New_Republic_Special_Forces "New Republic Special Forces") to Akiva. The group agreed to Ackbar's proposal. As a result, Akiva became one of the first Outer Rim worlds to join the New Republic.[[18]](#cite_note-Aftermath-18)

#### Juggling ideals and reality[]

:   "*I know. You're not wrong. And you are a hero, and you helped us all be the heroes needed to get to this point. But such passion and idealism have to be tempered by reality. This is a government. It has a lot of moving pieces.*"
:   ―Mon Mothma debating with Princess Leia[[107]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-107)

In [5 ABY](/wiki/5_ABY "5 ABY"),[[108]](#cite_note-Life_Debt_Date-108) Chancellor Mon Mothma continued to preside over the New Republic's war against the Galactic Empire. The New Republic liberated more worlds from the Empire including Akiva and [Arkanis](/wiki/Arkanis "Arkanis"). Chancellor Mothma and Princess Leia later traveled to the oceanic planet of [Velusia](/wiki/Velusia "Velusia") to meet with [Grand Vizier](/wiki/Grand_Vizier "Grand Vizier") [Mas Amedda](/wiki/Mas_Amedda "Mas Amedda"), who was still struggling to rule the Imperial capital of Coruscant; which was in the throes of a [civil war](/wiki/Coruscant_civil_war "Coruscant civil war"). On the atoll [Kolo-ha](/wiki/Kolo-ha "Kolo-ha"), the Grand Vizier tried to surrender but the Chancellor refused to accept his surrender and ordered him to find a way to secure the Empire's surrender. If he tried to walk away, Mothma and Leia threatened to have him tried for war crimes.[[107]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-107)

Later, Chancellor Mothma presided over a meeting to discuss the state of the New Republic. During the meeting, Mothma urged her fellow leaders to focus on winning more member worlds. When her adviser Hostis Ij advocated finding new lines of food, fuel and other vital supplies, [Auxi Kray Korbin](/wiki/Auxi_Kray_Korbin "Auxi Kray Korbin") interjected that a stronger military was not the solution. When Leia entered the room, Chancellor Mothma greeted her and apologized for not inviting her. Mothma was aware that Leia was under stress since her husband Han Solo had embarked on a mission to rescue Chewbacca.[[107]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-107)

When Leia tried to lobby for ships and resources to be sent to [liberate](/wiki/Liberation_of_Kashyyyk "Liberation of Kashyyyk") Kashyyyk, Mothma praised her for her idealism but warned her that the New Republic was preoccupied with trying to govern the galaxy. Despite Leia's pleas, Mothma reasoned that the New Republic lacked sufficient resources and manpower to liberate Kashyyyk. Frustrated, Leia stormed off.[[107]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-107)

#### The faux peace offer[]

:   "*The show is part of it. The galaxy is a myriad, wonderful place. It is home to such wild miscellany. Present her is individuality. Something the Empire, I feel, has missed. If there is to be any kind of treaty, it is vital we preserve what makes life in this galaxy special. It is critical we preserve all of what you will see on display. All ways of existence. All the choices for all of us.*"
:   ―Chancellor Mothma hosting Grand Admiral Sloane[[107]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-107)

 [![Chancellor Mothma entered into peace negotiations with Grand Admiral Sloane](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ab/WoTG-RaeSloane-Stormtroopers.png/revision/latest?cb=20230822225526) [![Chancellor Mothma entered into peace negotiations with Grand Admiral Sloane](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ab/WoTG-RaeSloane-Stormtroopers.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230822225526)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ab/WoTG-RaeSloane-Stormtroopers.png/revision/latest?cb=20230822225526) 

Chancellor Mothma entered into peace negotiations with Grand Admiral Sloane

 

After Admiral Ackbar liberated the planet [Kuat](/wiki/Kuat "Kuat") and the strategically important [Kuat Drive Yards](/wiki/Kuat_Drive_Yards "Kuat Drive Yards"), Chancellor Mothma contacted the Admiral via hologram to inform him and Princess Leia that she had received a communication request from the Operator, a shadowy Imperial operative who had been supplying vital intelligence on Imperial movements to Admiral Ackbar. Grand Admiral [Rae Sloane](/wiki/Rae_Sloane "Rae Sloane"), the leader of the Empire, then joined the conversation and claimed that she was the Operator. While Leia and [Commodore](/wiki/Commodore "Commodore") Kyrsta Agate expressed skepticism, the New Republic leaders including Mothma took an interest in Sloane's offer to discuss peace with the New Republic.[[107]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-107)

Believing that victory was imminent, Mon Mothma agreed to submit Sloane's offer to the Senate. As a gesture of trust, Sloane offered to have the [Imperial–Republic peace talks](/wiki/Imperial%E2%80%93Republic_peace_talks "Imperial–Republic peace talks") take place on Chandrila with minimal guard. Mothma accepted Sloane's offer and agreed to remain in contact with her using a special channel. Later, Chancellor Mothma and Senator Organa greeted a hundred prisoners that the former New Republic pilot [Norra Wexley](/wiki/Norra_Wexley "Norra Wexley") and her team had liberated from [Ashmead's Lock](/wiki/Ashmead%27s_Lock "Ashmead's Lock") prison on Kashyyyk with the help of Han Solo. Unknown to Mothma and her fellow leaders, the real Operator was [Fleet Admiral](/wiki/Fleet_Admiral "Fleet Admiral") Gallius Rax, who was ruling the Empire from behind the scenes. In secret, Rax was planning to attack Chandrila using the liberated Ashmead's Lock prisoners to assassinate the New Republic leadership. He used inorganic bio-chip implants to control the former captives.[[107]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-107)

A month following the rescue of the Ashmead's Lock prisoners, the Galactic Senate agreed to Sloane's offer for peace talks. Mothma timed the peace talks to take place after the [Liberation Day](/wiki/Liberation_Day_(New_Republic) "Liberation Day (New Republic)") celebrations to mark the liberation of the Ashmead's Lock prisoners. To prevent any obstacles to the peace talks, the Chancellor ordered the New Republic military to refrain from making any incursions into Kashyyyk. As a sop to Leia, Mothma agreed to raise the matter of Kashyyyk's liberation in her meeting with Sloane. Her pragmatism failed to sway the idealistic Leia, who insisted that the Wookiees' freedom and dignity was non-negotiable.[[107]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-107)

After Grand Admiral Sloane landed at spaceport in her shuttle, Chancellor Mon Mothma and several New Republic soldiers, guards, and officials received the Grand Admiral and her entourage. Mothma then took her Imperial guests to the [Old Gather-House](/wiki/Old_Gather-House "Old Gather-House") and the [Senate Plaza](/wiki/Senate_Plaza_(Chandrila) "Senate Plaza (Chandrila)") to watch the Liberation Day festivities, which featured artistic and musical displays by the various member worlds and species in the New Republic. When Sloane made a disparaging remark about [Gabdorin](/wiki/Gabdorin "Gabdorin") [music](/wiki/Music "Music"), Mothma responded that the New Republic represented everybody in the galaxy.[[107]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-107)

Following the parade, Chancellor Mothma began a speech praising the liberated Ashmead's Lock prisoners for their contributions to the Rebellion. Before she could conclude her speech, the prisoner [Brentin Lore Wexley](/wiki/Brentin_Lore_Wexley "Brentin Lore Wexley") tried to shoot her but was restrained by his wife Norra. The other prisoners also opened fire on the various New Republic officials present. Mothma survived the attack due to Norra's quick response but suffered serious injuries. Commodore Agate was badly scarred while General Madine and Adviser Hostis Ij were rumored to be dead. The attack ended any prospect for resolving the Galactic Civil War through diplomacy. In response, Fleet Admiral Rax ordered the Imperial fleets to assemble at [Jakku](/wiki/Jakku "Jakku").[[107]](#cite_note-Life_Debt-107)

#### In the thick of politics[]

:   "*The chancellor has made herself clear. This meeting is over. We will see you all on Nakadia.*"
:   ―Auxi speaking on behalf of Chancellor Mothma[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

In the months after the attack on Chandrila, Chancellor Mon Mothma chaired a meeting of the [Committee for Imperial Reallocation](/wiki/Committee_for_Imperial_Reallocation "Committee for Imperial Reallocation"), which dealt with redistributing the resources of the fallen Empire. Growing weary, Mothma advocated ending the meeting early and delaying it till next month. Mothma was preoccupied with efforts to move the Senate and her office to the [Mid Rim](/wiki/Mid_Rim_Territories "Mid Rim Territories") world of [Nakadia](/wiki/Nakadia "Nakadia"). Despite Senator [Ashmin Ek](/wiki/Ashmin_Ek "Ashmin Ek")'s protests, Auxi Kray Korbin reiterated the Chancellor's position and adjourned the meeting.[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

Before leaving, the [Hosnian Prime](/wiki/Hosnian_Prime "Hosnian Prime") councilman [Sondiv Sella](/wiki/Sondiv_Sella "Sondiv Sella") asked Mothma about her arm. Mothma replied that her arm was still recovering and that she was taking therapy exercises. Sella also promised to lobby the committees to fruition and to support her for the upcoming election. After the senators had departed, Mothma and Auxi chatted about her popularity ratings and the matter of appointing a new adviser to replace the late Hostis Ij, who had perished during the attack on Chandrila. After reflecting on her tense rivalry with the [Orishen](/wiki/Orishen "Orishen") Senator [Tolwar Wartol](/wiki/Tolwar_Wartol "Tolwar Wartol"), Mon asked Auxi how she could convince the Senate to vote for her again in the upcoming election.[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

Auxi reassured Mothma that she was doing the right things by apportioning resources and infrastructure for worlds afflicted by the Empire and the vacuum of leadership. While Mothma had kept the military strong, she had not tried to enforce her will on a weakened galaxy. When Auxi mentioned the liberation of Kashyyyk, Mon respond that Kashyyyk had been a complicated matter since the Senate had resisted their involvement but that Leia had gotten involved. Mothma had approved the clandestine action because it had been successful.[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

When Auxi opined that Kashyyyk was a victory for them, Mothma reminded her that they had secured this win by defying the will of the Senate. Auxi responded that leadership could mean defiance but Mothma countered that Palpatine was defiant. Auxi reminded her that Princess Leia was defiant but was not Palpatine. Auxi then raised the matter of law and order. Before Mothma could respond, one of the Chancellor's protocol droids [R-K77](/wiki/R-K77 "R-K77") informed her of an urgent meeting request from Princess Leia. The droid added that the request was a [Code K-one-zero](/wiki/Code_K-one-zero "Code K-one-zero") request, which meant something of the utmost importance.[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

#### News from Jakku[]

:   "*Yes, but we have to do this right. We don't even know what this is yet. Why this planet? How much of a fight are we to expect? We want this to be be the Empire's last stand. Not ours.*"
:   ―Mon Mothma responding to the news of the Empire's retreat to Jakku[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

Princess Leia had received news from [Temmin Wexley](/wiki/Temmin_Wexley "Temmin Wexley") and [Sinjir Rath Velus](/wiki/Sinjir_Rath_Velus "Sinjir Rath Velus") that the Imperial remnants had relocated to the [Inner Rim](/wiki/Inner_Rim_Territories "Inner Rim Territories") world of Jakku. Upon arriving at Leia's domicile, she asked Temmin to recount everything that he had told Leia. Temmin explained that the Empire was on Jakku and that a lot of ships were in orbit including at least one [Super Star Destroyer](/wiki/Super_Star_Destroyer "Super Star Destroyer"). Sinjir then interjected that his friends Norra Wexley and [Jas Emari](/wiki/Jas_Emari "Jas Emari") were on Jakku. When Chancellor Mothma remarked that the situation was fraught, Sinjir appealed to her to send military forces to save his friends and Temmin's mother.[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

Chancellor Mothma pointed out that their mission to Jakku had been unauthorized. When Leia responded that she had authorized the mission, Mothma countered that she did not have the Senate's authority and that hunting Rae Sloane was the jurisdiction of the Senate. When Leia urged Chancellor Mothma to seize the opportunity to attack, the Chancellor responded that they had to be careful that they had all the facts before proceeding to Jakku. The Chancellor then explained that she was unable to authorize the deployment of military forces to Jakku without consulting the Senate. She also warned the others not to speak of their meeting.[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

Unknown to Chancellor Mothma and the others, their conversations were being tapped by Senator Tolwar Wartol, who had planted a listening device in Leia's [nanny droid](/wiki/Nanny_droid "Nanny droid") [T-2LC](/wiki/T-2LC "T-2LC"). Wartol leaked the news of the Imperial presence on Jakku to [HoloNet News](/wiki/HoloNet_News "HoloNet News") and took the opportunity to attack Mothma for being secretive and indecisive. After watching the HoloNet news broadcast, Chancellor Mothma conferred with her adviser Auxi and Admiral Ackbar. Ackbar supported her by pointing out that she had been wise for not disclosing the information immediately since she it for less than a standard day.[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

Mon Mothma then realized that Senator Wartol had a leak or a spy. After reflecting on the situation, Mothma commented that her setback was one one the "necessary bumps and scratches of a growing democracy." In response to Wartol's leak, she instructed Auxi to contact HoloNet News to give her statement. Admiral Ackbar also agreed to send a [probe droid](/wiki/Probe_droid "Probe droid") and a scout ship to the Jakku system to gather intelligence on the Imperial presence. Leia urged her advisers to remain vigilant for traitors in their midst.[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

#### The derailed resolution[]

:   "*It's just—it must be hard, being you. Under siege from every direction.*"  
    "*Yes. It is hard. But we persevere. Like the Rebel Alliance before us, like the New Republic now. We persevere.*"
:   ―Tracene and Mon Mothma[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

Later, Chancellor Mothma met with the HoloNet News journalist [Tracene Kane](/wiki/Tracene_Kane "Tracene Kane") and the [Sullustan](/wiki/Sullustan "Sullustan") cam-operator [Birt](/wiki/Birt "Birt") to deliver her statement to the press. In her speech, Mothma reiterated that she had become aware of reports that the Empire had retreated to Jakku. She reassured the public that the military had sent a scout ship and a probe droid to confirm this information. While acknowledging rumors that the Imperial remnants had relocated to Jakku, she announced that she had convened an emergency session of the Senate in order to mobilize the armed services. After giving her press statement, Mon chatted with Tracene. When Tracene expressed sympathy for her predicament, Mon responded that the New Republic would persevere like the Rebel Alliance.[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

That night, Chancellor Mothma gave a speech to the Galactic Senate urging them to authorize military intervention on Jakku. She presented data from the probe droids and the scout ship *[Oculus](/wiki/Oculus "Oculus")* as evidence that the bulk of Imperial forces had relocated to Jakku. Following the speech, Mothma retreated to her office to recuperate. While chatting with Auxi, Admiral Ackbar entered the office to inform her that the vote had failed. Unknown to Mothma and her advisers, the [Black Sun](/wiki/Black_Sun "Black Sun") and [Red Key](/wiki/Red_Key_Raiders "Red Key Raiders") crime syndicates were plotting to prolong the fighting. They had coerced or bribed five senators into voting against Mothma's motion. At the request of Princess Leia, Sinjir contracted the services of his [slicer](/wiki/Slicer "Slicer") friend [Conder Kyl](/wiki/Conder_Kyl "Conder Kyl"). Conder found Wartol's listening device in T-2LC. After learning about the listening device, Chancellor Mothma decided to pay Senator Wartol a visit.[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

#### Meeting a political rival[]

:   "*You did do it. You sabotaged the vote.*"  
    "*I admit to nothing. I will not give life to your conspiratorial fancies.*"
:   ―Mon Mothma confronting Senator Wartol[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

Making use of Chancellor Mothma visited Senator Wartol's [Ganoidian tri-deck cruiser](/wiki/Ganoidian_tri-deck_cruiser "Ganoidian tri-deck cruiser") just as he was preparing to depart for Nakadia. When Wartol's Orishen guards tried to block her, Mothma warned them that turning her away with the threat of violence would not look good for the Senator. Chancellor Mothma managed to convince Senator Wartol to allow her to join him on his trip to Nakadia under the pretext of meeting with him. While the two shared a meal of roasted [Nektods](/wiki/Nektod "Nektod"), Wartol asked about the purpose behind her visit since they were political opponents. Mothma replied they both had shared interests and wanted what was best for the galaxy.[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

In private, Chancellor Mothma asked Wartol about her failed resolution to attack the Empire's fleet on Jakku, which had failed by five votes. Wartol tried to deny his involvement but Chancellor Mothma pointed out that the five dissenting senators Ashmin Ek, [Rethalow](/wiki/Rethalow "Rethalow"), [Dor Wieedo](/wiki/Dor_Wieedo "Dor Wieedo"), [Grelka Sorka](/wiki/Grelka_Sorka "Grelka Sorka"), and [Nim Tar](/wiki/Nim_Tar "Nim Tar") had voted with him in the past and worked with him in various councils and caucuses. While Wartol had voted in favor of military intervention, Mothma observed that the five senators had taken their cues from him in the past.[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

As the conversation dragged on, Mothma theorized that Wartol had convinced the five other senators to oppose the resolution while voting for it. When Mothma accused Wartol of sacrificing his principles, the Orishen responded that his people knew the meaning of sacrificing their world so that the Empire would not subjugate them. Despite Wartol's rhetoric about sacrifice, Mothma pointed out that he was sacrificing the New Republic's war efforts so that he could conquer the New Republic. She added that by manipulating the five senators, Wartol was sacrificing the safety of the galaxy.[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

When Wartol accused her of being a weak and indulgent leader, Mothma insinuated that he had sabotaged the vote. Wartol reiterated his denial and accused her of indulging in conspiracy theories. In response, Mothma presented the listening device that Conder had extracted from T-2LC. When Wartol denied planting the bug, Mothma countered that he knew that the Empire was on Jakku and that he had ordered the guards to stop Sinjir and Temmin from leaving on the *[Millennium Falcon](/wiki/Millennium_Falcon "Millennium Falcon")*. When Wartol reiterated his denial, Mothma vowed to fight him at the next election.[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

#### Intrigue on Nakadia[]

:   "*Those who vote no: Recognize that you are marked. You will be marked as cowards at best and traitors at worst.*"
:   ―An excerpt from Chancellor Mothma's speech urging the Galactic Senate to send military forces to Jakku[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

Wartol retorted that her re-vote was scheduled to take place on Nakadia in less than twelve hours and that she had little time to scramble the votes that she needed. However, Mothma then revealed a card up her sleeve; she had smuggled in a small [pta fruit](/wiki/Pta_fruit "Pta fruit"). Since Nakadia was an agrarian world, it was classified as a Class A protected planet by the New Republic. Senator Wartol's yacht was prevented from landing by the Nakadian authorities since the pta fruit was considered a biosecurity hazard. Thus, Mothma succeeded in delaying the re-vote.[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

This gave her allies Han Solo, Sinjir, Temmin, Conder Kyl, and the former New Republic soldier [Jom Barell](/wiki/Jom_Barell "Jom Barell") enough time to track down the five senators. Despite Conder being kidnapped by the Red Key syndicate, Jom managed to capture Rethalow. Rethalow revealed that the Black Sun and Red Key syndicates had coerced and bribed the senators into opposing Mothma's resolution. Sinjir and his team managed to defeat the criminal syndicate's plot by rescuing Conder and Senator [Nim Tar's child](/wiki/Nim_Tar%27s_child "Nim Tar's child"). Posing as the Chancellor's adviser, Sinjir managed to convince the five senators to change their votes by offering to pardon them.[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

Meanwhile, Chancellor Mothma and Senator Wartol finally cleared the Nakadian customs and addressed the press. To delay the proceedings, Mothma feigned a limp as they entered the [Quarrow Senate house](/wiki/Quarrow_Senate_house "Quarrow Senate house"). During the session, Mothma gave a short but angry speech urging the senators to vote for intervention on Jakku. She urged them not to hesitate in ending the Empire. While Mothma feared that she sounded like Palpatine, Auxi reassured her that it was a great speech. Mothma was relieved when Auxi later informed her that her vote had passed.[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

#### A new adviser[]

:   "*Yes, your reputation in that regard precedes you, Sinjir. But another reputation is beginning to form and grow: You are even more incisive with your tongue than you are with your violence. You can be alarmingly convincing, as evidenced by what you said to Senator Rethalow. And further how you manipulated those senators into giving me their vote. I need someone like that. Auxi is a most excellent adviser in matters political, but I need a cynic. Someone who distrusts the system—who maybe even despises it. And I also need someone who can play the game and get me what I want. That someone is you.*"
:   ―Chancellor Mothma recruits Sinjir as her new adviser[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

Following the Galactic Senate's decision to send military forces to Jakku, Chancellor Mothma returned to Chandrila. After learning of Sinjir's exploits, she secured a meeting with the former Imperial [loyalty officer](/wiki/Loyalty_officer "Loyalty officer")–turned New Republic operative. When Sinjir asked to go to Jakku, Mothma countered that he was not a soldier and that his talents were better applied elsewhere. Mothma offered to hire Sinjir as her new adviser to complement Auxi. She pointed out that she needed a cynic who distrusted the system. After some discussion, Sinjir accepted her job offer.[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

Chancellor Mothma then sent Sinjir on his first assignment to deliver a small basket of pta fruits to her political rival Senator Wartol. Sinjir and his partner Conder visited the Orishen senator and caught him red-handed trying to trigger a remote-controlled bomb. While they failed to stop Wartol from [detonating](/wiki/Assassination_attempt_on_Mon_Mothma "Assassination attempt on Mon Mothma") the bomb, the two managed to overpower the rogue Senator, who readily admitted to plotting to kill the Chancellor. The bomb destroyed Chancellor Mothma's office on Chandrila. While her adviser Auxi was killed, Mothma survived because she was outside the building.[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

Despite the loss of her friend Auxi, Mothma refused to allow grief to cloud her judgment. With the [Battle of Jakku](/wiki/Battle_of_Jakku "Battle of Jakku") ending in the New Republic's favor, Chancellor Mothma received word that Grand Vizier Mas Amedda had escaped Imperial captivity and was suing for peace. Chancellor Mothma accepted Amedda's offer and enlisted the help of her advisers Sinjir, Sondiv Sella, and Princess Leia. She arranged for the Imperial surrender to take place on Chandrila in the crystal cliffs north of Hanna City under an ancient [tintolive tree](/wiki/Tintolive_tree "Tintolive tree").[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

#### Galactic Concordance[]

:   "*Hope through agitation. The light glows stronger when we struggle.*"
:   ―Mon Mothma, following the signing of the Galactic Concordance[[109]](#cite_note-Empire's_End-109)

During the meeting, Mas Amedda signed both the [Imperial Instruments of Surrender](/wiki/Imperial_Instruments_of_Surrender "Imperial Instruments of Surrender") and the [Galactic Concordance](/wiki/Galactic_Concordance "Galactic Concordance"). Per the terms of the Instrument of Surrender, the Empire and the various splinter factions were ordered to cease fighting. Mon Mothma also issued a further declaration designating all surviving Imperial military officers as war criminals. Non-combatant functionaries within the Empire were given conditional pardons provided they complied with the articles of the Galactic Concordance. Grand Vizier Amedda was pardoned and tasked with leading the [Coruscant's provisional government](/wiki/Coruscant%27s_provisional_government "Coruscant's provisional government").
